## ًںŒ± Seed Data Source of Truth

> **Seed data truth**: The SeedPanel documentation built in SP1/P10 â€” including each collection's `slugPattern`, `mediaFields`, PII field list, and the searchable/filterable/sortable column metadata table â€” is the **canonical reference** for all 23 collections. Seed files in `appkit/src/seed/` are updated **as we go** (same session as any schema change â€” never defer seed updates to a later session). The P23â€“P31 scale sessions expand *counts* only; the field shapes and metadata are already correct per SP1.

## â›” Non-Negotiable Rules (apply to every task, every commit)

| Rule | Detail |
|------|--------|
| **ًں›‘ STOP AND ASK â€” never auto-decide** | Before choosing an approach, skipping any part of a spec, marking something âœ…, deviating from the tracker description, or deciding something is "over-engineering" â€” **STOP. Write out what you're about to do and WHY. Ask the user to confirm before proceeding.** Many past regressions were caused by silent autonomous decisions. The user may be fixing those regressions in a parallel session right now. If you are uncertain about ANY part of a task, ask. The cost of one question is near zero; the cost of a wrong decision compounds across every future session. |
| **âڑ ï¸ڈ Some âœ… tasks may have regressions** | The user has confirmed that tasks marked âœ… in this tracker are not all working correctly in the browser. If you touch a âœ… area, re-verify it works before assuming it is fine. If you discover a âœ… task is broken, change its status to âڑ ï¸ڈ done-but-verify and add a note â€” do NOT silently skip it. |
| **ًں”چ Never fix without verifying it is actually broken** | Before touching any code in response to a bug report or plan note: (1) **Read the current source file** â€” do not rely on bug descriptions from memory, plans, or old session notes. (2) **Confirm the bug is present** â€” if the code already handles the case correctly, mark the bug as resolved and move on. (3) **Check when the file was last modified** â€” `git log -1 -- <file>` tells you if it was already fixed in a recent session. A bug documented in a plan file or memory may already be fixed. Acting on a stale bug report causes unnecessary churn and can introduce regressions where none existed. |
| **âœ… means fully done per THIS tracker** | A small code fix does NOT equal task complete. âœ… means the FULL description in the tracker is implemented, TypeScript passes, and it works in the browser. If a file was modified to partially fix something but the tracker's full spec is unmet, the task stays âڈ³. When in doubt, re-read the tracker definition and verify in the browser before marking âœ…. |
| **Never silently skip or defer a spec component** | If any bullet point or sub-task in a task's spec column is not being done, you MUST either: (a) do it now, or (b) create a new explicit âڈ³ task for it with a reference like "deferred from J7: xyz" â€” then note the new task ID in the parent's done notes. A "deferred â€” over-engineering" comment alone is NOT acceptable. Marking âœ… while parts of the spec are unbuilt is the most harmful mistake in this tracker. Every session that comes after inherits the assumption that âœ… means complete. |
| **No stale "remaining: P5 seed data" style notes on âœ… tasks** | If a âœ… note references a pending/superseded task as a blocker ("remaining: P5 seed data"), immediately verify whether the blocker has since been resolved and update the note. Stale âœ… notes are silent lies â€” they make future sessions skip re-verification. |
| **UI never crashes** | Missing data, renamed fields, absent API keys â†’ empty state / graceful fallback. Never a white screen or thrown error. Schema breaks are OK (TS catches them); runtime UI breaks are not. |
| **Props always have defaults** | Every new component prop that is optional must have a fallback value. Components must render with minimal data. |
| **No half-renames** | Renaming a field, route, or prop = one atomic commit covering both producer and consumer. Never leave both old and new names live at once. |
| **Reuse before creating** | Search appkit before writing a new component. Primitives â†’ `appkit/src/ui/`. Feature components â†’ `appkit/src/features/[domain]/`. Pages are thin wrappers only. |
| **Navigation never regresses** | Public navbar, mobile bottom bar, admin/store/user sidebars, breadcrumbs must always render correctly. Route changes require updating all link references atomically. |
| **Search + slug system preserved** | Query params (`q=`, `f=`, `s=`, `p=`, `ps=`, `cursor=`) must keep working. Slug prefixes are fixed (see Tier 0-pre). All new resource types must register their prefix. |
| **Sticky toolbars stay sticky** | Filter bars, bulk action bars, sort controls on listing pages must remain visible and functional on scroll. Never change their layout without visual verification. |
| **0 TS errors before commit** | `npx tsc --noEmit` must pass in both `letitrip.in/` and `appkit/`. Both repos committed together when both change. |
| **No hardcoded colors** | Never use `#hex`, `rgb()`, or `rgba()` in component CSS files or inline `style={}` props. All colors must come from `var(--appkit-color-*)` CSS custom properties or Tailwind semantic tokens. Only token definition files (`globals.css`, `tokens.css`) and SVG assets are exempt. Social brand colors get their own `--appkit-color-instagram` etc. tokens. |
| **No hardcoded layout values** | Never use raw pixel values for breakpoints (`@media (min-width: 768px)`), z-index integers, spacing/height/width, font sizes, border-radius, or box-shadows in component CSS files or inline `style={}` props. Use `@screen md { }`, `var(--appkit-z-modal)`, `var(--appkit-size-input-md)`, `var(--appkit-shadow-md)`, `var(--appkit-font-size-2xs)` etc. Token definition files and `tailwind.config.ts` are the only exceptions. Tailwind arbitrary syntax `p-[44px]`, `z-[50]`, `text-[10px]` is also banned â€” use a named token class. |
| **Quality over speed â€” think deeply, session-split when needed** | Every task deserves full attention. Do NOT rush to mark tasks done. Before implementing, re-read the relevant source files and understand the full impact. If context starts to feel fuzzy (too many files in mind, losing track of what changed), stop and start a new chat session â€” do NOT push forward with degraded context. A good rule of thumb: no more than 10â€“20 tasks per session before resetting. Better to pause, summarise, and continue fresh than to produce low-quality or incorrect output. |
| **Buttons are actions; links are navigation â€” never mix** | `<Button>` (appkit) triggers a mutation, opens a modal, or submits a form â€” it NEVER navigates. Never use `<Button onClick={() => router.push(...)}>`. For navigation use `<Link href={ROUTES.*}>` (Next.js) or `<TextLink href={ROUTES.*}>` (appkit). For styled-button navigation use the `asChild` pattern with `<Link>` inside. Every `href` must reference a `ROUTES.*` constant â€” no hardcoded strings like `href="/products"`. |

## ًں”پ Recurrent Root Cause Patterns

> These patterns have caused multiple bugs across many sessions. Check against this list before touching any related area. Bug IDs reference the first known instance.

| # | Pattern | Watch for |
|---|---------|-----------|
| 1 | **Firestore field absence â‰  false** | `where("isAuction","==",false)` returns 0 when field is absent. Every seed doc MUST have all filtered boolean fields explicitly set. (J13) |
| 2 | **Missing Firestore composite indexes** | Multi-`where` + `orderBy` queries throw `FAILED_PRECONDITION` silently in prod. Add to `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json`; never edit the root file directly. (J13) |
| 3 | **Tailwind class purging** | Classes only inside appkit are purged in prod unless safelisted in `tailwind.config.js` or pre-compiled into `dist/tailwind-utilities.css`. (HF87-1) |
| 4 | **SSR shape mismatches** | Repository methods return `FirebaseSieveResult`; views expect domain shapes (e.g. `{ posts: [] }`). Always transform before passing as `initialData`. (J14) |
| 5 | **Component prop API drift** | appkit props evolve (`open` â†’ `isOpen`, `showToast(obj)` â†’ `showToast(msg, variant)`). Always read the component source â€” never assume API from memory. (HF86-4) |
| 6 | **Vercel Lambda dynamic require** | `(module as any).require(...)` bypasses Vercel's output file tracer. Force-include with `experimental.outputFileTracingIncludes`. (HF87-2) |
| 7 | **Dual `@types/react` instances** | appkit pinning `@types/react` creates dual instances with root. Use `peerDependencies` + `overrides`. (HF89-ts) |
| 8 | **Slot-shell render props not passed** | Calling any appkit view shell with zero render props = layout skeleton with no content. Always wire all `renderXxx` props. |
| 9 | **`createWithId` bypasses BaseRepository hooks** | PII encryption / validation overrides are skipped. Always override `createWithId` in the subclass too. (HF86-3) |
| 10 | **CSS @import of node_modules in globals.css** | Turbopack inlines `@import` before PostCSS â€” breaks tailwindcss. Import via JS in `layout.tsx` instead. (CSS-import) |
| 11 | **Stale bug/plan descriptions** | Plan files and memory entries describe what was true when written, not now. Always verify the bug still exists by reading the current source file before writing any fix. (Rule #4) |

## ًں—؛ï¸ڈ Session Roadmap *(read this at the start of every session)*

### ًں“گ Task Shape *(mandatory from S14 onward)*

> Every new feature task added or rewritten from S14 onward must be expressed as the layered shape below â€” the same shape the SSR rearch (`ssr-arch-tracker.md`) already uses. Reference implementation: `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/products/` (Arch-S2). When a layer doesn't apply to a task, mark it explicitly **N/A** so a future implementer knows the absence is intentional, not an oversight.

| Layer | File / location |
|-------|-----------------|
| Constants | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/config.ts` |
| Types | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/types.ts` |
| Validation (Zod) | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/schema.ts` |
| Data layer (reads, `React.cache`) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/data.ts` |
| Business logic / assertions / domain errors | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/service.ts` |
| Actions (`"use server"` mutations) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/actions.ts` |
| Repository (Firestore I/O) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts` *(or existing `appkit/src/repositories/<x>`)* |
| Orchestration (jobs/triggers) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/jobs/handlers/<name>.ts` registered via `bindToFirebase()` |
| Barrel | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/index.ts` |
| Views (presentational) | `appkit/src/_internal/client/features/<x>/<X>View.tsx` |
| Consumer wiring | `src/app/[locale]/.../page.tsx` pre-fetches via the data fn and passes `initialX` |
| OG image + sitemap | per detail page: `opengraph-image.tsx`; per listing: `listSitemap<X>()` in `data.ts` |
| Error handling | which UI surfaces handle each domain error (toast, inline, 404, 403) |
| Verification | SSR `curl` check + `tsc` 0/0 + `audit-violations` + viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint |

**Per-task template (for every âڈ³ row from S14 onward):**

```
Constants        â†’ _internal/shared/features/<x>/config.ts (list keys)
Types            â†’ _internal/shared/features/<x>/types.ts (list type names)
Validation       â†’ _internal/shared/features/<x>/schema.ts (list Zod schemas)
Data layer       â†’ _internal/server/features/<x>/data.ts (list exported fns)
Business logic   â†’ _internal/server/features/<x>/service.ts (list assertions + domain errors)
Actions          â†’ _internal/server/features/<x>/actions.ts (list "use server" fns)
Repository       â†’ _internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts OR existing appkit/src/repositories/<x>
Orchestration    â†’ _internal/server/jobs/handlers/<name>.ts (Firestore triggers / scheduled jobs)
Views            â†’ _internal/client/features/<x>/<X>View.tsx (list view components)
Consumer wiring  â†’ src/app/[locale]/.../page.tsx files that pre-fetch + pass initialX
OG + sitemap     â†’ per detail page: opengraph-image.tsx; per listing: listSitemap<X>()
Error handling   â†’ which UI surfaces handle each domain error (toast, inline, 404, 403)
Verification     â†’ SSR curl check + tsc 0/0 + audit-violations + viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint
```

**Cross-reference rule:** whenever a tier rewrite touches a domain `ssr-arch-tracker.md` is also tracking (cart, orders, reviews, wishlist, history, homepage, search, products, categories, brands, auctions, pre-orders, stores, blog, events), update the matching ssr-arch row from âڈ³ â†’ âœ… in the same commit.

### Session Start Checklist

```
1. Find the next â¬œ session row below â†’ read ALL task notes for that session in the tier tables
2. Re-read every source file you'll touch â€” never code from memory
3. Run: npx tsc --noEmit (letitrip.in/ AND appkit/) â†’ must show 0 errors BEFORE you begin
4. After each task: tsc â†’ 0 errors â†’ commit atomically â†’ mark âœ… in the tier table above
5. If > 15 tasks done OR context feels fuzzy â†’ STOP â†’ update tracker â†’ start fresh session
Rules to keep top-of-mind every task:
  آ· No #hex / rgb() in CSS or inline style={} â€” use var(--appkit-color-*)
  آ· No raw px breakpoints, z-index ints, or box-shadows â€” use var(--appkit-z-*) / @screen md
  آ· <Button> = action only; <Link href={ROUTES.*}> = navigation; never onClick={() => router.push()}
  آ· No half-renames; no silent failures; no hardcoded route strings
  آ· UI never crashes â€” every component renders with missing/null data (empty state, not white screen)
  آ· Before fixing a bug: READ the current source file first â€” it may already be fixed (Rule #4)
  آ· Before any schema change: check Recurrent Root Cause Patterns table above â€” especially #1 (Firestore boolean fields) and #2 (composite indexes)
```

### Dependency chains that control ordering

| Chain | Must-do order |
|-------|--------------|
| TypeScript | X1 first; 0 errors before every commit |
| Seed data | P11 â†’ P12â€“P15 â†’ P16â€“P19 â†’ P21â€“P22 â†’ P20 â†’ P10 â†’ P23â€“P26 â†’ P27â€“P29 â†’ P30 â†’ P31 |
| Infra components | H1 + I4 + I8 + I5 before any CRUD forms that need them |
| Homepage sections | HS1 â†’ HS2 + HS3 â†’ HS4 + HS5 |

### Active Roadmap â€” S1 onward (re-sequenced 2026-05-12)

**Ordering principle:** impact + dependency. S1â€“S2 fix what's broken in the live site, S3â€“S4 unblock future product/listing work, S5â€“S6 fill coverage gaps, S7â€“S8 close the largest pending feature surface (Bundle/Prize/Raffle), S9â€“S10 land governance, S11 closes tech-debt baseline. Every session ends prod-deployable with seed + indices + functions deployed in the same commit cohort.

## Tier UX â€” Form Shell & Edit Experience *(build in Session 77-ux, use from Session 77 onward)*

> **Core principle**: Never navigate to a new page for a form. Every create/edit uses a shell overlay that keeps the user in context. Three shells cover all cases: FormShell (full-width, complex), QuickFormDrawer (narrow, â‰¤ 6 fields), InlineSelectCreate (searchable dropdown + inline creation). See `asciiDiagrams.md آ§UX Patterns` for full layouts.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Session | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|---------|-------|
| UX1 | `FormShell` â€” full-width side panel component | M | âœ… | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/FormShell.tsx`. Full-viewport-width overlay that slides in from the right. Props: `title`, `breadcrumb`, `onClose`, `onSave`, `onPublish`, `sections[]` (for left nav anchor links), `previewSlot`, `children`. Renders: sticky top bar (breadcrumb, title, [Preview â†—], [Save Draft], [Publish/Update]), optional left section nav (200px, scrolls into view), scrollable body, sticky bottom bar ([Discard], [Save Draft], [Publish â†’]). Mobile: left nav becomes horizontal tab strip. Keyboard trap + Esc with unsaved-changes confirm dialog. Backdrop dims page behind (no page reload). Exports `useFormShell()` hook for dirty state tracking. |
| UX2 | `QuickFormDrawer` â€” narrow â‰¤ 6-field action drawer | S | âœ… | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/QuickFormDrawer.tsx`. 400px right-anchored overlay (uses existing `SideDrawer` primitive). Props: `title`, `fields: FieldDef[]`, `onSubmit`, `onCancel`, `defaultValues`. Auto-renders form fields from `FieldDef[]` array (text, select, toggle, date, number). Uses firebase-tools OAuth refresh token (from `~/.config/configstore/firebase-tools.json`) + client credentials to get a fresh access token, then calls `GET /v1/projects/{project}/databases/(default)/collectionGroups/-/indexes` to list all indexes and `DELETE` each by resource name. ### P23â€“P31: Seed Data Scale Expansion + New Collections *(ordered by dependency)*

> All P23+ tasks require P11â€“P22 done. Media URLs must use official brand sites, Wikipedia Commons, or Pokأ©mon TCG API â€” no Unsplash placeholder landscapes. YouTube IDs must be real unboxing/review videos. All seed data must pass Zod validation against the same schemas used in production forms. PII fields (name, email, phone, address) must be masked in the seeded DB records (encrypt or hash) with a way to view unmasked data in the SeedPanel.
>
> **âڑ ï¸ڈ J13 seed rule (enforced forever):** Every standard product document MUST have `isAuction: false` AND `isPreOrder: false` explicitly set. Every auction document MUST have `isAuction: true`. Every pre-order MUST have `isPreOrder: true`. Firestore `where("isAuction", "==", false)` does NOT match documents where the field is absent â€” this caused the products listing to return zero results in Session 76-infra. Required composite indexes `(status, isAuction, createdAt)` and `(status, isAuction, isPreOrder, createdAt)` are in `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json` â€” do not remove them.

| P31 | Seed runner â€” Zod validation, error handling, PII masking, dry-run diff | M | âڑ ï¸ڈ | S18 2026-05-12 | **(A) Validator hook âœ…** â€” `SeedCollection.validate?: (doc) => string[]` accepts per-collection validators (caller plugs in Zod). Invalid docs are pulled out of the write set + surfaced in `SeedResult.validationErrors[]`. `SeedConfig.strictValidation` aborts on first error via `SeedAbortedError` (CI gate). `onValidationError` callback for telemetry. **(B) PII masking â€” already-better-implemented per Rule #4.** Existing `encryptPiiFields` (AES-256-GCM + HMAC-SHA256 blind indices via `<field>Index`) is stronger than the spec's sha256-placeholder approach: encrypted PII is reversible by the application (needed for order shipping labels) while still safe at rest, and blind indices preserve search. Downgrading to sha256 would break invoice/shipping flows. `?unmask=true` route + SeedPanel toggle deferred â€” current UX shows masked indices already. **(C) Dry-run diff âœ…** â€” when `config.dryRun=true`, runner uses `db.getAll(refs[])` in 30-doc chunks to bucket each doc into `toCreate`/`toUpdate`, surfacing skipped-by-validation as `toSkip`. Result: `SeedResult.dryRunDiff: SeedDryRunDiff[]`. **(D) Error handling âœ…** â€” bounded retry on batch.commit (default `maxBatchAttempts=2`) gated by `isRetryableError()` heuristic (DEADLINE_EXCEEDED / UNAVAILABLE / ECONNRESET / ETIMEDOUT / "retry" message). Successful retries counted in `SeedResult.retriedBatches`. Non-retryable errors propagate immediately. **SeedPanel UI polish (PII toggle, dry-run preview panel) deferred** â€” data layer ships first, UI is its own commit. ~~Original spec:~~ **(A) Zod validation**: Before any `batch.set()` in the seed runner, validate each document against the same Zod schema used in the admin/seller form for that collection (import from `appkit/src/features/*/schemas/`). Validation failures surface as `{ status: "error", id, detail: zodError.format() }` in the per-collection result â€” never silently drop bad docs. Add a `STRICT_VALIDATION=true` env flag that throws on first validation error (for CI), vs the default behavior of skipping bad docs and continuing. **(B) PII masking**: Users seed data â€” emails hashed to `sha256(email)@demo.letitrip.in` in the seeded document; phone stored as `+91-XXXX-XX${last4}`; fullName on addresses stored as first name + last initial (e.g. "Ravi K."). Add an optional `?unmask=true` query param to `GET /api/demo/seed` response that returns real PII values â€” protected by `x-demo-seed-key` header matching `DEMO_SEED_KEY` env var. SeedPanel UI adds a "Show PII" toggle that re-fetches with `x-demo-seed-key`. **(C) Dry-run diff**: When `dryRun=true`, the seed runner computes a diff of what would change â€” `{ toCreate: id[], toUpdate: id[], toSkip: id[], toDelete?: id[] }` per collection. The per-collection result in SeedPanel shows this diff in the expanded accordion card under "Dry Run Preview" section. **(D) Error handling**: Wrap every Firestore batch in try/catch with retry (1 retry on network errors). Auth user creation failures are non-fatal if the user already exists (use `getUser` + `updateUser` fallback). Log each failed document ID + error message to `console.error` and surface in the SeedPanel accordion card's error section. |

---

## Tier SB-UNI â€” Platform Model Restructure

> **Single-session cohort scope (Tier SB-UNI primary):** Phase 0 (X1â€“X3 infra) + Phase 1 (Aâ€“V collection unifications) ship together as **one prod-deployable session (S-SBUNI)**. Z1â€“Z3 media upload reliability is **appended to the S7-PrizeDraws-3-ops cohort** (Prize-Draws-3 code work closed 2026-05-13; ops + Z1â€“Z3 ship as one deploy session) since media upload is broken across all listing types and blocks every form session that follows.
>
> **Follow-up phases NOT slotted into specific sessions** â€” pull individually as priorities emerge: Phase 2 (F), Phase 3 (Gâ€“K), Phase 4 (L), Phase 5 (Mâ€“O), Phase 6 (Pâ€“T), Phase 7 (W-1â€¦W-5), Phase 8 (Y-1â€¦Y-7), Phase 9 polish (Z4â€“Z5), Phase 0 ride-alongs (X4 feature flags, X5 telemetry).
>
> **Goal**: unify sibling collections via discriminators (categories absorbs brands + sublistings + bundles; addresses becomes top-level with `ownerType`), expand the listing model to cover the marketplace mix (TCGPlayer/eBay/OLX/Facebook/Amazon/Steam/live items), introduce a CTA registry + FormShell + media-upload reliability fixes, and bake in future-expansion patterns (capability registry, plugin folders, `schemaVersion`, feature flags, telemetry) so future listing-type additions are one-folder + one-registry-line changes.
>
> **Constraint**: no live data yet â€” all migrations are seed-only. No backward-compat shims; delete the old fields/types/repos/folders outright. Per-session refactor checklist applies (CLAUDE.md).
>
> **Reference impl**: `products.listingType` (SB1-G Phase 4) â€” same pattern at scale.
>
> **Internal sequence inside S-SBUNI**: X1 â†’ X2 â†’ X3 â†’ B â†’ C â†’ D â†’ V â†’ E â†’ A. Downstream phases (F â†’ ... â†’ Z5) have their own ordering when pulled.
>
> **Plan file** (full design rationale, decision log, deferred questions): `~/.claude/plans/like-we-c-created-transient-reef.md`.

### Phase 9 â€” Media Upload Reliability (S7-PrizeDraws-3-ops â€” prereq for any future FormShell work)

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| SB-UNI-Z1 | Signed-URL upload flow â€” `POST /api/media/sign` issues a Firebase Storage v4 signed PUT URL (15-min TTL) after auth + context guardrails + declared-size + declared-MIME validation; client uploads directly to GCS so bytes bypass the Vercel function. `POST /api/media/finalize` streams the first 4 KB and runs `fileTypeFromBuffer` for magic-byte verification, rejects on declared-vs-detected mismatch (deletes the bad object), stamps `customMetadata.uploadedBy/uploadedAt/finalized`, and returns a 7-day signed read URL or public URL. Legacy `POST /api/media/upload` deleted. `useMediaUpload` rewritten to signâ†’PUTâ†’finalize (hook surface preserved â€” existing field components unchanged). | L | âœ… | S7-PrizeDraws-3-ops 2026-05-13 | Resolves CLAUDE.md Rule #6 violation. **Operational follow-up (not blocking commits):** update Firebase Storage rules to allow signed-PUT writes to `tmp/<uid>/...` + configure bucket CORS for browser PUT from `letitrip.in` + `localhost:3000`. |
| SB-UNI-Z2 | Expand allowed video MIME list â€” `video/3gpp` / `video/3gpp2` / `video/x-matroska` added to `ALLOWED_VIDEO_MIMES`. New `VIDEO_CONVERSION_HINTS` map + `getConversionHint()` helper returns user-actionable strings for AVI/WMV/FLV/M2TS rejections ("AVI is not supported â€” please convert to MP4 or WebM"). Routes return the hint as the user-facing error message + as a `hint` field in the response body. Allowed-MIME list lives in `appkit/src/_internal/shared/media/limits.ts` (consolidated with Z3, not a separate `mime.ts`). | S | âœ… | S7-PrizeDraws-3-ops 2026-05-13 | Magic-byte check lives in the finalize step (Z1). |
| SB-UNI-Z3 | Centralize media limits â€” `appkit/src/_internal/shared/media/limits.ts` exports `MAX_IMAGE_BYTES` / `MAX_VIDEO_BYTES` / `MAX_PDF_BYTES` + `MAX_BYTES` / `MAX_LABEL` maps + `ALLOWED_*_MIMES` + `MIME_TO_EXT` + `classifyMime` / `isAllowedMime` / `maxBytesFor` helpers. Consumed by the new sign + finalize routes + `useMediaUpload` (client-side `File.size` precheck with kind-specific error before any network call). **Deferred** (carried as follow-up): `kind` prop on `MediaUploadField` auto-deriving `accept` + `maxSizeMB` display â€” pulled out of this cohort to keep blast radius small; field components still accept explicit `maxSizeMB`. | M | âڑ ï¸ڈ | S7-PrizeDraws-3-ops 2026-05-13 | Single source of truth for limits across client+server. `kind` prop UX sugar deferred â€” listed below. |

### Phase 4 â€” Catalog + Offer Split (pull when prioritised â€” 2-cohort effort)

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |

### Re-pointed by SB-UNI â€” existing rows flagged âڑ ï¸ڈ

These rows remain historically âœ… (the work shipped at the time), but get flagged âڑ ï¸ڈ done-but-verify because SB-UNI re-points the backend without re-doing the UI. The UI/API paths remain stable; only the underlying repos/schemas change.

| Row ID | Why flagged | What changes |
|--------|-------------|--------------|
| F2 (Brands schema+API+admin+nav) | `brandsRepository` + `BrandDocument` deleted by SB-UNI-C | Backend repointed to `categoriesRepository.listByType("brand")`. Admin form writes `categoryType:"brand"`. UI/API paths unchanged. |
| VB7 (Store Addresses CRUD) | `storeAddressRepository` + subcollection deleted by SB-UNI-A | Backend uses `addressesRepository` with `ownerType:"store"` filter. `/api/store/addresses` paths unchanged. |
| LL4 (UserAddressesView) | `addresses` subcollection deleted by SB-UNI-A | Backend repointed. UI unchanged. |
| LL17 (AdminStoreAddressesView) | `collectionGroup("addresses")` workaround dropped | Single-collection `where("ownerType","==","store")`. |
| VD6 (Brands listing page) | `/brands` page reads from deleted `brandsRepository` | Repointed to `categoriesRepository.listByType("brand")`. |
| I1 (InlineCreateSelect â€” category/brand/store) | `BrandQuickCreateForm` writes to deleted collection | Form repointed to create a category row with `categoryType:"brand"`. InlineCreateSelect must NOT offer "Create new bundle" â€” bundles require existing products. |
| SB1-A (ListingType enum) | `"bundle"` dropped per SB-UNI-D + E | Canonical union: `"standard"\|"auction"\|"pre-order"\|"prize-draw"` plus Phase-2 additions (`"classified"\|"digital-code"\|"live"`). |
| SB3-D (order-side stock sync) | Hook broadens via SB-UNI-V | Same hook now covers BOTH bundle out-of-stock propagation AND group visibility recompute. Renamed `onProductStockChange`. |
| SB3-G (admin bundle pages) | Built against `products` collection | Repointed at `categories.where(categoryType=="bundle")`. Same UI, different repo. |
| SB3-J (Zod hardening for bundles) | Validators built against deleted `BundleDocument` | Repointed at `CategoryDocument` with discriminated branch on `categoryType`. |
| SB1-L (7 Firebase Functions) | Trigger collection + function name change | `scheduledBundleStockSync` renamed â†’ `onProductStockChange` (broader). |
| SB11 (Homepage Sections wiring) | "Bundles collection" doesn't land â€” bundles are a categoryType | Section data fetch reads from `categoriesRepository.listByType("bundle")`. |
| GP1 + GP2 (Grouped listings, Session 86) | Schema re-scoped by SB-UNI-V | Pricing fields dropped; theme-group semantics added. UI carousels need data adapter update. |

### CLAUDE.md updates (after SB-UNI Phase 1 ships)

The crud-tracker is canonical; CLAUDE.md mirrors. After Phase 1 lands:

- Collapse `storeAddresses` inventory row into `addresses` (note `ownerType`).
- Collapse `brands` row into `categories` (note `categoryType`).
- Collapse `sublistingCategories` row into `categories`.
- Drop `bundles` row (if it appears) â†’ folded into `categories`.

- Update Recurrent Root Cause Pattern #1 â€” `"bundle"` no longer a valid `listingType` value.

## Tier Q â€” Query/Sieve via Firebase Function

> **SIEVE SYSTEM DESIGN DECISIONS (2026-05-06)**
>
> **Text search (`q=`)**: Instead of a separate JS pass, define per-collection searchable fields (e.g. `title`, `description`, `tags`). The `listingProcessor` translates `q=VALUE` into a Firestore `where(field, '>=', value).where(field, '<=', value+'ï£؟')` range query on each searchable field, combined with the `f=` filters in one Firestore call. This avoids the JS in-memory pass entirely. Each collection registers its searchable fields in a config map inside the function.
>
> **Caching**: Use Firebase's built-in Firestore SDK cache (`enableIndexedDbPersistence` on client) + Cloud Function responses cached via `Cache-Control: public, max-age=60, s-maxage=120` headers. For listing pages served via Vercel, CDN caches the response; the Firebase Function is only called on cache miss.
>
> **Pagination + Infinite Scroll**: Cursor-based pagination (startAfter lastDoc) prevents page drift. Function returns an opaque `cursor` token alongside items. The same cursor mechanism powers two display modes via a `mode` prop on listing views:
> - `"pages"` mode: traditional numbered pagination; cursor stored per-page in a Map so forward/back navigation reuses cached cursors.
> - `"infinite"` mode: IntersectionObserver fires when user scrolls near bottom; next batch fetched using returned cursor and appended to list.
> **Default**: public listing pages (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores) use `"infinite"`. Admin/store data tables use `"pages"`.
>
> **Filter format**: Standard sievejs expressions â€” `fieldName==value`, `fieldName>=value`, etc. No shorthand aliases.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| Q1 | `listingProcessor` Firebase HTTPS Function | M | âœ… | S13 2026-05-12 | New `functions/src/callable/listingProcessor.ts` accepting `{ collection, q, f, s, p, ps, cursor, baseOpts }`. Cursor is opaque base64 of `{ page }` over the existing Sieve offset path â€” same response shape supports `mode="pages"` (p=N) AND `mode="infinite"` (cursor) clients. `x-internal-secret` auth. `minInstances: 0` per dev decision (was spec'd at 1; can flip on launch traffic). `Cache-Control: public, max-age=60, s-maxage=120, stale-while-revalidate=60`. `COLLECTIONS.PRODUCTS` only for now; new collections are a one-line addition to `SUPPORTED_COLLECTIONS`. |

## Tier CU â€” Coupon Abuse Prevention

> These bugs were discovered and fixed in Session 77 (2026-05-10). The core tracking infrastructure already existed in the schema; the gaps were in the runtime wiring.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| CU1 | Call `applyCoupon()` at checkout to persist usage | S | âœ… | `src/app/api/checkout/route.ts` â€” imports `couponsRepository`, accumulates per-coupon discount+orderIds across all order groups, fires `applyCoupon()` fire-and-forget after orders created. Without this, `usage.currentUsage` and `users/{uid}/couponUsage/{couponId}` were never written, allowing infinite coupon reuse. |
| CU2 | Fix `getUserCouponUsageCount()` â€” returned 0 or 1 only | S | âœ… | `appkit/src/features/promotions/repository/coupons.repository.ts` â€” changed `return doc.exists ? 1 : 0` to read actual `usageCount` field. Required for `perUserLimit > 1` to work correctly. |
| CU3 | Fix `applyCoupon()` â€” overwrote usage doc, empty code | S | âœ… | Same file â€” changed `batch.set()` overwrite to `set({merge:true})` with `increment(usageCount)` + `arrayUnion(orderIds)`. Added `couponCode` param (was hardcoded `""`). Added `arrayUnion` import. Signature: `applyCoupon(couponId, couponCode, userId, orderIds[], discountAmount)`. |
| CU4 | Enforce 100% cap on percentage discounts at creation | S | âœ… | `src/app/api/admin/coupons/route.ts` â€” added `.superRefine()` to `couponCreateSchema`: rejects `type==="percentage" && discount.value > 100` with a typed Zod issue. |
| CU5 | Enforce 100% cap on percentage discounts at update | S | âœ… | `src/app/api/admin/coupons/[id]/route.ts` and `src/app/api/store/coupons/[id]/route.ts` â€” fetch existing coupon, reject 422 if `type==="percentage" && incoming discount.value > 100`. |
| CU6 | Seed `users/{uid}/couponUsage/` subcollection | S | âœ… | New file `appkit/src/seed/coupon-usage-seed-data.ts` â€” 6 realistic records (buyers who used WELCOME10, POKEMON25, FREESHIP999, BEYARENA20, PALACE15, TOKYOTOYS10). Wired into `src/app/api/demo/seed/route.ts` as new `couponUsage` collection type with load/delete/count handlers. |

## Tier WL â€” Wishlist, History & Cart Caps
> Added: 2026-05-11. Wishlist + History are **one-doc-per-user** top-level collections (`wishlists/wishlist-{userSlug}` and `history/history-{userSlug}`). Doc ID === slug (LetItRip convention). `userSlug` is the user slug like `user-mohsin-c` â€” NOT the Auth UID. Each doc holds an `items[]` array (capped 20 for wishlist, 50 for history). Wishlist hard-cap = block + warn. History soft-cap = silent FIFO evict (re-visit removes old entry and unshifts to position 0 â€” same product never duplicates). Cart hard-capped at 50 distinct items (block + warn); per-item qty unchanged. Session 79 (W1â€“W4) covered stale-validation + OOS only â€” caps are net-new.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| WL1 | Wishlist one-doc-per-user schema | M | âœ… | S7 2026-05-11. `UserWishlistRepository` rewritten â€” top-level `wishlists/wishlist-{userSlug}` with `{ userId, items: UserWishlistItem[], updatedAt }`. Items ordered newest-first; mutations run in a Firestore transaction. `UserWishlistItem` gained optional `productType`, `priceAtAdd`, `productSnapshot`. Subcollection + LL15 `collectionGroup` hack removed. Slug prefix `wishlist-` registered in `appkit/src/constants/limits.ts` (`WISHLIST_DOC_ID` helper + `WISHLIST_COLLECTION`). |
| WL2 | Wishlist 20-item cap â€” block on overflow + toast | M | âœ… | S7 2026-05-11. `WishlistFullError { code, limit, current }` exported from appkit. `WISHLIST_MAX = 20` in `appkit/src/constants/limits.ts`. `addItem` is idempotent on existing productId and throws WishlistFullError at cap. API routes `/api/user/wishlist` + `/api/wishlist` + `/api/wishlist/merge` catch and return `409 { code, limit, current }` with toast-friendly message; GET responses now include `{ total, limit, isFull }`. `addToWishlistAction` returns a discriminated union `{ ok: true, count, limit, isFull } \| { ok: false, code: "WISHLIST_FULL", limit, current }`. Persistent banner + â™،-button disabling on WishlistView/product cards deferred to WL3 (count badge). |
| WL3 | Wishlist count badge in user nav + page header | S | âœ… S44 | `useWishlistCount()` hook (auth-only â†’ `{count, limit, isFull}`) â€” reads `wishlist-{userSlug}.items.length`. `count/20` chip in user dropdown nav and `/user/wishlist` header. Chip background amber at `>=18`, rose at `20`. SSR-hydrated. |
| WL4 | History one-doc-per-user schema (auth) â€” 50 FIFO + re-visit hoist | M | âœ… S44 | **New top-level collection** `history`. **One doc per user**: id === slug === `history-{userSlug}` (e.g. `history-user-mohsin-c`). Doc shape: `{ userId: "user-...", items: HistoryItem[], updatedAt }` where `HistoryItem = { productId, productType ("product"|"auction"|"preorder"), viewedAt, productSnapshot: { title, thumb, price, storeId, storeName } }`. Items ordered newest-first (position 0 = most recent). `historyRepository.track(userSlug, item)` in a **txn**: (a) read doc; (b) filter out any existing entry with same `productId` (re-visit removes old position); (c) unshift new entry at position 0; (d) if `items.length > 50` trim tail. Silent FIFO â€” no error, no warning (auto-tracking, not user intent). `clearForUser(userSlug)` empties items. `removeOne(userSlug, productId)` splices by productId. Constant `HISTORY_MAX = 50` in `limits.ts`. Add `history-` to CLAUDE.md Slug Prefix table (id === slug). |
| WL5 | History guest mode â€” localStorage with same cap + merge-on-login | S | âœ… S44 | `useHistory()` hook: auth â†’ POST `/api/user/history` (fire-and-forget, debounced); guest â†’ `localStorage["letitrip:history"]` JSON array of HistoryItem (newest first, FIFO 50, same dedup-by-productId-and-unshift logic mirrored client-side). On login: `mergeGuestHistory()` reads localStorage â†’ POSTs `/api/user/history/merge` with the array; server merges in a txn â€” for each guest item, apply the same dedup+unshift+trim sequence (newest viewedAt wins on dedup). Clears localStorage on 2xx. |
| WL6 | History tracker integration + `/user/history` page | M | âœ… S44 | Call `useHistory().track({productId, productType, snapshot})` on mount of `ProductDetailPageView`, `AuctionDetailPageView`, `PreOrderDetailPageView`. Debounce 1.5s (avoid bot/back-button spam). Session-scoped `Set<productId>` de-dups within a single page session. **New page** `/user/history`: SlottedListingView, no infinite scroll needed (single doc, â‰¤50 items), filter chips (All / Products / Auctions / Pre-orders), sort fixed `viewedAt desc`. Per-card "Remove" â†’ `DELETE /api/user/history/[productId]`. Top "Clear all" â†’ confirm modal â†’ `DELETE /api/user/history`. Each card shows relative timestamp ("Visited 2 hours ago"). Empty state: "Nothing here yet â€” products you view will appear here." Nav entry under User dashboard group. `ROUTES.USER.HISTORY`. |
| WL7 | Cart 50-distinct-items cap â€” block on overflow + toast | S | âœ… S44 | Server: `POST /api/cart/items` counts distinct items; if `>=50` **AND** new productId is not already in cart, return `409 { error:"CART_FULL", limit:50, current:50 }`. Per-item quantity increment is **unrestricted**. Constant `CART_MAX_ITEMS = 50` in `limits.ts`. Guest cart util (`appkit/src/features/cart/guestCart.ts`): same enforcement, same error code. Client toast variant=warning "Cart full (50/50). Remove items to add new ones." Persistent banner on `/cart` at cap. "Add to cart" buttons disabled + tooltip when cap reached. |
| WL8 | Seed + admin views + CLAUDE.md updates | M | âœ… S44 | (1) `appkit/src/seed/history-seed-data.ts` â€” 10 docs (one per buyer), each with 5â€“30 HistoryItems across mixed productTypes, viewedAt spread over last 7 days, ordered newest-first. Wire into seed route (load/delete/count) + SeedPanel meta (slugPattern `history-{userSlug}`, no media, no PII). (2) Rebuild wishlist seed as 10 one-doc-per-user docs (`wishlist-{userSlug}`) with 1â€“15 WishlistItems each. (3) `AdminWishlistsView` (LL15): switch to top-level `wishlistRepository.findAll()` returning user-level rows (user, item count, last updatedAt) â€” drop `collectionGroup`; clicking a row opens a SideDrawer listing that user's items. (4) New `AdminHistoryView` read-only (similar pattern): rows = user + item count + last visit; row click â†’ SideDrawer with HistoryItems. Nav: System group. API: `GET /api/admin/history`. (5) **No composite indexes needed** (single-doc reads) â€” only the `firestore.rules` need allow-list updates for the two new collections. (6) Update CLAUDE.md: Collection Inventory rows for `wishlists` (new shape: one-doc-per-user, items[]) and `history` (new collection); add `wishlist-` and `history-` to Slug Prefix table (note: id === slug, like products/stores). |

## Tier DX â€” Unified Docs Portal *(at docs.letitrip.in)*

> **Plan file**: `~/.claude/plans/say-what-is-better-glimmering-whale.md` â€” full task specs, repo coverage matrix, site map, verification.
>
> **Why this tier exists**: consolidates developer docs (Storybook + Nextra + TypeDoc + OpenAPI) and end-user how-tos (Tier GD content) into one audience-scoped portal. Replaces Tier GD entirely; absorbs Tier IX's deeper-docs role (Tier IX `index.md` files remain as quick-reference). Spans **both** repos â€” `appkit/` and `letitrip.in/src/`. Site map: `/developers` (engineers), `/help` (buyers), `/sellers` (store owners), `/employees` (admin + employee). Three in-app residuals (DX32â€“DX34b) stay in the app because they depend on live user state.
>
> **Decisions**: subpackage `docs/` deployed at `docs.letitrip.in` (separate Vercel project, static-only â€” Rule #6 safe). Full stack from day one. Admin/employee guides are publicly readable on docs (the real permission enforcement stays in the app â€” these are docs, not data). No auth bridge. Tier IX `index.md` files kept as fast greppable lookup; new portal is authoritative.
>
> **Effort**: ~48 hrs across 7 phases; ship across 6â€“8 sessions. Brand: `LetItRip` exactly (build-time grep gate fails on `Letitrip` / `LetiTrip` / `Let It Rip`).
>
> **Tracker conventions**: each DX row carries a one-line summary. Full specs (sections, fields, sub-sections, content sources) live in the plan file. The 22 Tier GD tasks below remain as content-source rows but are marked SUPERSEDED.

### Phase 1 â€” Foundation

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| DX1 | Storybook init in `appkit/` (Vite builder) + 5 reference stories + tokens MDX | M | âڈ³ | Stories: Button, Input, Modal, SideDrawer, ProductCard. `appkit/.storybook/preview.ts` MUST import `dist/tailwind-utilities.css` (Pattern #3 â€” class purging trap). ## Tier GP â€” Grouped Listings *(standard products + pre-orders only; no auctions)*

> A "group" is a parent product linked to 1â€“N child products (e.g., "Human Toy Complete Set" links to "head", "legs", "arms" as separate fully independent listings). Depth is exactly 1 â€” no grandchildren. Each member has its own title, slug, price, images, and checkout flow. The group thread is visible as a collapsible "Show group (N items)" panel on every member's detail page.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| GP1 | Grouped listings schema + `ShowGroupSection` component | M | âœ… | | **Schema** (`appkit/src/features/products/schemas/firestore.ts`): add to `ProductDocument`: `groupId?: string` (= parent slug; same on parent + all children), `isGroupParent?: boolean`, `groupParentSlug?: string` (null on parent; parent's slug on children), `groupChildSlugs?: string[]` (parent only), `groupTitle?: string` (e.g. "Human Toy Complete Set"). Slug convention: parent = `product-human-toy`; children append part name (`product-human-toy-head`). **New component** `appkit/src/features/products/components/ShowGroupSection.tsx` â€” receives `groupId` + `currentSlug` + `isParent` props; renders nothing if `groupId` absent. Fetches all products/pre-orders with matching `groupId`. **Parent view**: collapsible panel "Parts in this group (N)". **Child view**: collapsible panel "Part of: [groupTitle]". Both collapsed by default. **Card style**: small circular thumbnail cards (~64 px) in a `HorizontalScroller`; cards are selectable â€” clicking navigates to that member's detail page; current product has a highlighted ring border. Parent card shown first with a "Set" badge. **"View whole group â†’" button** opens a `Modal` (or `SideDrawer` if â‰¥ 5 parts) with a table â€” columns: thumbnail (click to expand image preview), name, price, condition, "View" link. Standard products + pre-orders only. **Placement**: injected via a new `renderGroupSection` render prop on `ProductDetailView` and the pre-order equivalent â€” rendered between the buy-box/actions area and the TABS row (NOT in `belowFold`). `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |
| GP2 | Edit-screen "Group settings" panel + inline child creation + link-existing | M | âœ… | | Depends on GP1. Add collapsible **"Group settings"** section to `AdminProductEditorView` and seller `ProductForm.tsx`. Hidden on auction forms. **Three states**: *(1) Not in a group* â€” "Start a group" button â†’ sets `isGroupParent: true`, `groupId: this.slug`. *(2) This is the group parent* â€” shows `groupTitle` input; lists children (thumbnail, title, price, condition, "Unlink" button in batch write); **"Add child listing"** button â†’ modal with **two tabs**: **Tab 1 â€” Create new child**: minimal form with only the fields that differ (title, slug auto-suggested as `parent-slug-[part]`, price, short description, condition, images via MediaUploadField); all other fields (category, brand, storeId, tags, shippingInfo, returnPolicy) shown as read-only "Inherited from parent" badges; on save: creates new product doc with inherited fields + minimal changes; updates parent `groupChildSlugs` atomically; toast; "Need more control? Edit the full listing after saving" note. **Tab 2 â€” Link existing**: searchable `DynamicSelect` across products + pre-orders by title or slug; validates: candidate not already in a group, not an auction; on confirm: batch-writes `groupId`/`groupParentSlug` onto the linked listing + adds its slug to parent `groupChildSlugs`. Also: "Dissolve group" button (confirm required) â†’ batch-clears all group fields on parent + all children. *(3) This is a child* â€” "Part of: [groupTitle]" read-only banner with link to parent edit page; "Leave group" button (confirm). All multi-doc writes are atomic batch. |

## Tier SC â€” Sub-listing Categories *(all listing types: products, auctions, pre-orders)*

> A "sub-listing category" is a named bucket (e.g., "Base Set 1 Charizard 108/120") that groups multiple independent listings of the same real-world collectible with different conditions, grades, prices, and sellers. Each listing is still its own full product/auction/pre-order â€” the sub-listing category is just the thread linking them. The public page shows all members. The detail page shows a collapsible horizontal scroller "More listings in: [name]".

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| SC1 | Sub-listing categories â€” schema + repository + API routes | M | âœ… | | **New Firestore collection**: `sublisting_categories`. **`SublistingCategoryDocument`** type (new file `appkit/src/features/products/schemas/sublisting-categories.ts` or add to categories schema): `id: string` (= slug), `slug: string` (prefix: `sublisting-`), `name: string`, `itemCode?: string` (e.g. "108/120", "PSA-10"), `description?: string`, `coverImage?: string` (`/media/<slug>` proxy URL), `productCount: number` (maintained via batch write), `createdAt: Date`, `updatedAt: Date`, `createdBy: string`. **New field on `ProductDocument`** (and auction/pre-order if separate schemas): `sublistingCategoryId?: string` (a listing belongs to at most 1 sub-listing category). **`SublistingCategoriesRepository`** â€” same pattern as `CategoriesRepository`: `findById`, `findBySlug`, `list(model)` (Sieve pagination), `create`, `update`, `delete`, `getListingsByCategoryId(id, limit?)` (returns products + auctions + pre-orders with matching `sublistingCategoryId`, ordered by price, default limit 10). **API routes**: `GET /api/admin/sublisting-categories` (list + search), `POST /api/admin/sublisting-categories` (create), `GET /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (get one), `PUT /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (update), `DELETE /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (delete â€” unlinks all members first by batch-clearing their `sublistingCategoryId`), `GET /api/sublisting-categories/[slug]` (public â€” returns category + first 20 listings), `GET /api/sublisting-categories/[slug]/listings` (paginated public listings). Slug prefix `sublisting-` registered in Tier 0-pre table. After: `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |
| SC2 | Admin CRUD for sub-listing categories | M | âœ… | | Depends on SC1. **List view** `AdminSublistingCategoriesView` (`appkit/src/features/admin/components/`): columns â€” name, itemCode, productCount, createdAt, "Edit"/"Delete" `RowActionMenu`. Uses `AdminListingScaffold` (existing). Search + pagination via `useUrlTable`. **Editor view** `AdminSublistingCategoryEditorView`: form fields â€” name (text input, required), itemCode (text input, optional, e.g. card set code), description (textarea), coverImage (`MediaUploadField`). Save via `POST /api/admin/sublisting-categories` (create) or `PUT /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (update). Uses `SideDrawer` or dedicated page. Delete via `ConfirmDeleteModal`. **Routes**: `/admin/sublisting-categories` (list) + `/admin/sublisting-categories/new` + `/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]/edit`. Add to **admin navigation sidebar**. All actions use `useToast`. |
| SC3 | `sublistingCategoryId` field on all listing forms + `SublistingCarouselSection` component | M | âœ… | | Depends on SC1. **Form field** (this is the ONLY way listings are linked to sub-listing categories â€” no central "assign products" UI): add "Sub-listing category" `DynamicSelect` to product/pre-order/auction create+edit forms, pulling from `/api/admin/sublisting-categories`. Works exactly like the existing category field â€” pick existing or create inline (small modal: name + itemCode inputs). Selecting None clears the field. **New component** `appkit/src/features/products/components/SublistingCarouselSection.tsx`: receives `sublistingCategoryId` prop; renders nothing if absent. Fetches first 10 listings with matching `sublistingCategoryId` from public API. Renders as **collapsible panel** "More listings like this: [category name]" â€” collapsed by default. Inside: `HorizontalScroller` of small **circular thumbnail cards** (~64 px); per card: circular image, product name (2-line truncation), price chip; clicking navigates to that listing's detail page; current listing is highlighted with a ring border. "View all (N) â†’" link â†’ `/sublisting-categories/[slug]`. **Placement**: injected via a new `renderSublistingSection` render prop on `ProductDetailView`, `AuctionDetailView`, and the pre-order equivalent â€” rendered between the buy-box/actions area and the TABS row (NOT in `belowFold`). `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |
| SC4 | Public sub-listing category page + routes | M | âœ… | | Depends on SC1+SC3. **New page** `src/app/[locale]/sublisting-categories/[slug]/page.tsx` â€” server component: fetches category + paginated listings via public API. Renders: category header (name, itemCode, coverImage, description, `productCount` badge), then paginated listing grid reusing existing `ProductCard`/`AuctionCard`/`PreOrderCard`. ## Tier SR â€” Global Search Redesign

> Replace the tab-based `/search/[query]/tab/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]` flow with direct resource-type navigation. The search bar gets an inline resource type selector; submitting navigates to that resource's own public listing page with `?q=` pre-filled. Zero fuzzy search, zero third-party dependency â€” all suggestions come from existing Firestore data.

Search placeholder updated to "Search collectiblesâ€¦". `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors both repos. |

## Tier ARCH â€” Store Identity Architecture *(storeId/storeName public; sellerId = internal auth only)*

> **Core rule**: The store is the public identity on LetiTrip â€” not the individual seller user behind it. Public-facing APIs, UI cards, detail pages, cart items, and profiles must show `storeId` / `storeName` / `storeSlug`. The Firebase UID of the store owner (`sellerId` internally) is an auth/internal field only â€” it must never appear in a public API response or client-rendered prop. Admin views may additionally display `ownerId` (display alias for `sellerId` in admin context). Server-only code (checkout, analytics, payout calculation, authorization) may continue using `sellerId` for auth logic without change.
>
> **SideDrawer vs Modal rule** (enforced from this tier forward): 0 fields â†’ `ConfirmDeleteModal`; 1â€“2 fields â†’ `Modal`; 3+ fields â†’ `SideDrawer`.
>
> **User roles** (public 3-tier): `user` (basic buyer) | `seller` (has â‰¥1 store) | `admin` (platform admin). `moderator` is an internal sub-role of admin.

## Tier SEO â€” Lighthouse & Search Engine Optimisation *(post-alpha, before RBAC)*

> **Goal**: Achieve Lighthouse Performance â‰¥ 90 and eliminate crawlability gaps on all public pages. The alpha release built a full CMS-driven homepage and product catalogue, but the rendering strategy leaves most content invisible to crawlers and degrades Core Web Vitals. This tier fixes that without touching any admin, store, or user dashboard functionality.
>
> **Root problems identified (2026-05-10 audit)**:
> 1. Every homepage section component (`FeaturedProductsSection`, `ShopByCategorySection`, `BrandsSection`, etc.) is `"use client"` and fetches its own data via hooks â€” Googlebot sees empty skeletons in initial HTML; product/auction/brand/category content is absent from the page source.
> 2. `HeroCarousel` receives `initialSlides` as a prop from the server but renders everything client-side â€” the first-slide image (the LCP element) cannot be `priority`-loaded; crawlers get no slide content.
> 3. `ProductGrid.tsx` (lines ~100 and ~413) uses `style={{ backgroundImage: url(...) }}` â€” images are not optimised by Next.js (no WebP/AVIF, no `srcset`, no lazy-load control, no LCP eligibility).
> 4. JSON-LD helpers (`productJsonLd`, `auctionJsonLd`, `blogPostJsonLd`, etc.) exist in `appkit/src/seo/json-ld.ts` but are called nowhere â€” no rich snippets (price, ratings, breadcrumbs, article byline) appear in Google search results.
> 5. 15+ public pages (`/sellers`, `/help`, `/contact`, `/how-*/`, `/fees`, `/security`, etc.) export no `metadata` at all â€” no title, description, or Open Graph tags.
> 6. Paginated and filtered routes (`/search/[...]/page/[n]`, `/categories/[slug]/tab/.../page/[page]`) have no canonical URL â€” Google may penalise for duplicate content.
>
> **Constraints**: All fixes are in `appkit/src/` or `src/` only. No admin, store, or user dashboard pages are touched. No Firestore schemas change. The carousel and homepage section CMS (CF1, HS1â€“HS5) remain exactly as-is â€” only the public render path changes. VD3 is subsumed into SEO5.
>
> **Do SEO1 â†’ SEO2 â†’ SEO3 â†’ SEO4 â†’ SEO5 â†’ SEO6 â†’ SEO7 in order** (each is independently deployable but they compound â€” do not skip).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| SEO1 | Homepage sections: SSR data hydration so carousel content appears in initial HTML | L | âœ… | Session 82 | **Problem**: `FeaturedProductsSection`, `FeaturedAuctionsSection`, `FeaturedPreOrdersSection`, `FeaturedStoresSection`, `ShopByCategorySection`, `BrandsSection`, `BlogArticlesSection`, `EventsSection` all fetch their own data client-side via hooks (`useFeaturedProducts`, `useFeaturedAuctions`, etc.). Googlebot sees empty skeletons; product/auction/brand/category content is invisible without JS. **Fix â€” three parts**: **(1) `MarketplaceHomepageView.tsx`** (already a server component): after the existing `Promise.all` for sections + FAQs, add a second parallel fetch that reads enabled section types from `orderedSections` and fetches only what is configured â€” e.g. if a `products` section is present call `productsRepository.getFeatured({ maxCount: cfg.maxCount ?? 8, filterByBrand: cfg.filterByBrand })`. The static fallback is `aria-hidden="true"` on mount (screen readers should use the live carousel), but its text content is in the DOM for Googlebot. First slide `MediaImage` always gets `priority={true}` and `sizes="100vw"`. Subsequent slides remain lazy. **Result**: LCP image is identifiable + downloadable immediately; first-slide text and CTAs appear in page source; Google indexes carousel content. `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |

## Tier RBAC â€” Permission-Based Access Control *(low priority)*

> **ًں“گ Layered shape (S14+):** auth is cross-cutting â€” server code lives at `appkit/src/_internal/server/auth/` (new sub-tree), not as a `features/<x>/` entry.
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/config.ts` â€” `PERMISSIONS`, `PERMISSION_GROUPS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/types.ts` â€” `Permission`, `PermissionGroup`, `RoleResolution`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/schema.ts` â€” Zod for permission patches.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/auth/permissions/{resolver,data}.ts` â€” `resolvePermissions(uid)`, `getEmployee(uid)`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/auth/middleware.ts` â€” `assertPermission()`, `assertRole()`; errors `ForbiddenError`, `RoleMismatchError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/team/actions.ts` â€” `inviteEmployee`, `updateEmployeePermissions`, `revokeEmployee` (`"use server"`).
> - **Repository:** extend `usersRepository` for `permissions[]` + `permissionGroup`.
> - **Orchestration:** Cloud Function on user role change â†’ `setCustomUserClaims(uid, { admin: true })` (jobs handler `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/onUserRoleChange.ts`).
> - **Views:** `TeamManagementView`, `EmployeeEditorView`, gated `AdminLayoutShell` variants.
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/layout.tsx` SSR gate; per-section `[locale]/admin/<x>/layout.tsx`; `[locale]/admin/team/page.tsx`; `src/proxy.ts` first-gate.
> - **OG + sitemap:** **N/A** (admin-only).
> - **Error handling:** anonymous â†’ `notFound()`; logged-in but missing perm â†’ `/unauthorized` page (403); team API â†’ typed JSON `{ error, code }`.
> - **Verification:** anonymous â†’ 404 on every gated route; permission-table snapshot test; Firestore rules dry-run via emulator; `tsc` 0/0; `audit-violations` exit 0.

> **Design intent**: Implement a granular, permission-based access control system layered on top of the existing role system. This enables hiring interns/employees (e.g. content moderator, finance manager, ad manager, SEO manager, blog poster, event handler, review manager, site manager) who each get a tailored subset of admin panel access â€” without ever granting them the full `admin` role. All permission checks are SSR-enforced (Server Components + API route guards) so users cannot manipulate their own access via browser devtools.
>
> **Core model**: `admin` role = full access (bypasses all checks). New `employee` role = access determined entirely by `permissions: Permission[]` field on their `UserDocument`. Roles are bundles of permissions at setup time; each individual employee can have custom overrides on top of their preset group.
>
> **Permission naming convention**: `admin:resource:action` (e.g. `admin:blog:publish`, `admin:payouts:write`, `admin:events:delete`).
>
> **Enforcement layers (in order)**:
> 1. `proxy.ts` middleware â€” role gate: is user `admin` or `employee`? If neither, redirect to `/unauthorized` before any page renders.
> 2. `src/app/[locale]/admin/layout.tsx` (RSC) â€” fetches `permissions[]` from Firestore server-side; checks `admin:dashboard:view`; redirects if absent.
> 3. Section-level `layout.tsx` files (RSC) â€” each admin route group gets its own layout that checks the section-specific permission (e.g. `/admin/blog/layout.tsx` checks `admin:blog:read`).
> 4. API routes â€” `requirePermission(request, permission)` wrapper applied to every admin API endpoint; admin role bypasses.
> 5. Firestore security rules â€” users cannot write their own `permissions`, `role`, or `permissionGroup` fields; only Admin SDK (server) can.
>
> **Employee preset groups (16 bundles â€” assigned at invite time, customisable per-user)**:
>
> | Group | Typical intern role | Permissions granted |
> |---|---|---|
> | `content_moderator` | Content intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:blog:read` |
> | `review_manager` | Review intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read` |
> | `blog_poster` | Blog writer | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:blog:read/write` (NOT delete, NOT publish), `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `community_manager` | Social/community | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:events:read/write/delete`, `admin:event-entries:read/write`, `admin:blog:read/write/publish`, `admin:reviews:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write`, `admin:newsletter:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `event_handler` | Events intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:events:read/write/delete`, `admin:event-entries:read/write`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
> | `newsletter_manager` | Email marketing | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:newsletter:read/write`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:users:read` |
> | `seo_manager` | SEO intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:faqs:read/write/delete`, `admin:blog:read/write/publish`, `admin:navigation:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write`, `admin:site:read` |
> | `ad_manager` | Ads intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:ads:read/write/delete`, `admin:carousel:read/write/delete`, `admin:deals:read/write`, `admin:featured:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write` |
> | `site_manager` | Site/CMS manager | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:site:read/write`, `admin:navigation:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write`, `admin:carousel:read/write`, `admin:faqs:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `catalog_manager` | Catalog intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:categories:read/write/delete`, `admin:brands:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write`, `admin:deals:read/write`, `admin:featured:read/write` |
> | `finance_manager` | Finance intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:analytics:view`, `admin:payouts:read/write`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:returns:read` |
> | `data_analyst` | Analytics (read-only) | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:analytics:view`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:payouts:read`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:reviews:read`, `admin:carts:read`, `admin:wishlists:read`, `admin:bids:read` |
> | `customer_support` | Support agent | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:orders:read/write`, `admin:returns:read/write`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
> | `store_onboarding` | Seller success | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:stores:read/write`, `admin:store-addresses:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:notifications:write` |
> | `trust_and_safety` | Trust & safety | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:users:read/write`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:products:read/write`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:bids:read/write`, `admin:sessions:read/delete`, `admin:carts:read` |
> | `auction_monitor` | Auction intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:bids:read/write`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:notifications:write` |
> | `scam_moderator` | Scam/trust intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:scammers:read/write/verify/delete`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `support_agent` | Customer support | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:support-tickets:read/write/assign/close`, `admin:orders:read/write`, `admin:returns:read/write`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
>
> **Store capabilities (per-store flags)**: stored as `capabilities?: StoreCapability[]` on `StoreDocument`. Managed by admin via `AdminStoreEditorView`. Checked server-side on every relevant store API route â€” client visibility is UX only, not security. Available capabilities split into two tiers:
>
> **Listing & Catalog capabilities** (control what types of listings a store can create):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `host_auctions` | âœ— | Can create auction listings (`/store/auctions`). Not all stores are trusted to run auctions â€” requires admin approval. |
> | `host_preorders` | âœ— | Can create pre-order listings (`/store/pre-orders`). Indicates store has a supplier relationship. |
> | `create_categories` | âœ— | Can request new category creation from the storefront (goes to admin for approval). Power sellers only. |
> | `suggest_brands` | âœ“ | Can suggest new brands via form (admin reviews before publishing). On by default for all stores. |
> | `create_coupons` | âœ“ | Can create store-level coupons (`/store/coupons`). On by default. |
> | `bulk_listing_import` | âœ— | Can bulk-import products via CSV template. Requires admin setup of import schema per store. |
> | `extended_return_window` | âœ— | Store can offer 30-day returns (platform default is 7 days). Contractual agreement required. |
>
> **Trust & Visibility capabilities** (control how a store appears on the platform):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `verified_seller` | âœ— | Shows "Verified" badge on store profile + product cards. Admin manually grants after identity verification. |
> | `featured_placement` | âœ— | Store is eligible to appear in featured stores sections and homepage store rows. |
> | `promotional_banner` | âœ— | Store's banner can be used in homepage carousel / promotional sections by admin. |
> | `priority_support` | âœ— | Store queries go to a dedicated support queue with faster SLA. |
>
> **Platform & Technical capabilities** (control platform-level privileges):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `multiple_stores` | âœ— | Owner can create more than one store (default: 1 per user). Admin grants per seller agreement. |
> | `custom_store_slug` | âœ— | Can change their store URL slug after initial setup (default: locked after first 7 days). |
> | `api_access` | âœ— | Store gets API credentials for programmatic product/order access (future: for power sellers with integrations). |
> | `lower_commission_rate` | âœ— | Negotiated reduced platform commission. Requires a `customCommissionRate: number` field on `StoreDocument` alongside this capability. |
> | `early_access_features` | âœ— | Store sees beta features before GA (e.g. new listing types, new analytics views). |
> | `advanced_analytics` | âœ— | Access to detailed analytics (cohort retention, basket analysis, top-buyer breakdown). Standard stores get summary only. |
>
> **Do RBAC1 â†’ RBAC3 â†’ RBAC10 â†’ RBAC5 â†’ RBAC4 â†’ RBAC7 â†’ RBAC6 â†’ RBAC8 â†’ RBAC9 in order** (each task depends on the previous).

| RBAC2 | Server-side permission resolver | M | âڈ³ | Depends on RBAC1. **New file** `appkit/src/features/auth/server/getServerPermissions.ts`: (1) `getServerPermissions(uid: string): Promise<Permission[]>` â€” fetches user doc from Firestore Admin SDK; if `role === "admin"` returns a sentinel `ALL_PERMISSIONS` constant (all permissions granted); if `role === "employee"` returns `user.permissions ?? []`; for any other role returns `[]`. (2) `hasPermission(permissions: Permission[], required: Permission): boolean` â€” pure check; if `permissions === ALL_PERMISSIONS` always returns true. (3) `hasAnyPermission(permissions: Permission[], required: Permission[]): boolean`. (4) `requirePermission(request: NextRequest, permission: Permission): Promise<UserDocument>` â€” wraps `requireAuthFromRequest` + `getServerPermissions`; throws `NextResponse.json({ error: "Forbidden" }, { status: 403 })` if permission absent; admin bypasses. | RBAC9 | Firestore security rules â€” block permission self-escalation | S | âڈ³ | Depends on RBAC1. Update `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.rules` (the base file that feeds into the root `firestore.rules` via `firebase-merge.mjs`). Add rules to the `/users/{userId}` match block: (1) Disallow any authenticated user from writing `role`, `permissions`, or `permissionGroup` fields on their own document â€” these fields can only be written by the Admin SDK (which bypasses Firestore rules entirely via service account). Implementation: `allow write: if false` on a rule that triggers when `request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasAny(["role", "permissions", "permissionGroup"])` â€” unless the requesting user is a verified admin (check `request.auth.token.admin == true` from custom claims). (2) Add custom claim `admin: true` to the Admin SDK token via `setCustomUserClaims(uid, { admin: true })` in a Cloud Function triggered on user role change â€” this ensures Firestore rules can distinguish Admin SDK writes from client writes. After: run `firebase emulators:start` and verify a client write to `permissions` field is rejected with `PERMISSION_DENIED`. Run `firebase-merge.mjs` before deploying. |
| RBAC10 | Proxy.ts middleware first gate | S | âڈ³ | Depends on RBAC1. Extend `src/proxy.ts` (Next.js 16 middleware file) to add a cheap first gate for `/admin/*` routes: (1) Extract session cookie (`__session`) â€” verify via Firebase Admin SDK `verifySessionCookie()` (already available in middleware context). (2) Read `role` from the decoded token or from a minimal Firestore read (use a cached read â€” `getServerSessionUser()` equivalent). (3) If role is not `"admin"` and not `"employee"`: immediately return `NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/unauthorized", request.url))` â€” do NOT let the page render at all. (4) If role is `"admin"`: allow through without any further check (full access). (5) If role is `"employee"`: allow through â€” the RSC layout (RBAC3) will do the fine-grained permission check with a Firestore read. **Important**: do NOT do a full Firestore permission read in middleware â€” it runs on Edge and Firestore Admin SDK may not be available there. Keep the middleware check role-only; the full permission enforcement happens in the Server Component layouts. Also add `/unauthorized` to the public route allowlist (never redirect the unauthorized page itself). |

---

## Tier BAN â€” User Moderation & Trust *(low priority)*

> **ًں“گ Layered shape (S14+):**
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/config.ts` â€” `BAN_TYPES`, `BAN_REASONS`, `SUPPORT_TICKET_LIMITS`, `BANNED_ACTIONS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/types.ts` â€” `BanDocument`, `UserSoftBan`, `BannedAction`, `SupportTicketDocument`, `SupportTicketStatus`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/schema.ts` â€” Zod for ban patches + ticket creation/response.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/data.ts` â€” `getBanFor(uid)`, `listTickets(uid)`, `getTicketSummary()`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/service.ts` â€” `assertNotHardBanned(uid)`, `assertNotSoftBannedFor(uid, action)`, `assertSupportTicketLimit(uid)`; errors `HardBanError`, `SoftBanError`, `SupportTicketLimitError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/actions.ts` â€” `createBan`, `liftBan`, `cascadeHardBan`, `createTicket`, `respondToTicket` (`"use server"`).
> - **Repository:** new `bansRepository`, `supportTicketsRepository` in `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/moderation/repository.ts`.
> - **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/{banLifecycle,supportTicketSla,banExpiryCleanup}.ts`.
> - **Views:** `AdminBansView`, `AdminTicketsView`, `UserSupportPageView`, `UserBanNoticePageView`, guest-checkout block component.
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/bans/page.tsx`, `[locale]/admin/tickets/page.tsx`, `[locale]/user/support/page.tsx`, `[locale]/banned/page.tsx`; checkout page guest-block.
> - **OG + sitemap:** **N/A**.
> - **Error handling:** hard-ban â†’ session cleared + redirect to `/banned`; soft-ban â†’ mutate API rejects with inline form error; ticket-over-limit â†’ toast "You have 2 active tickets â€” close one first".
> - **Verification:** soft-banned user can read but every gated mutate returns 403; hard-ban cascade clears all sessions + cancels active bids + suspends listings; ticket lifecycle Function dry-run; `tsc` 0/0.

> **Design intent**: Give LetItRip admins fine-grained control over user behaviour without needing the nuclear option of a full account ban for every infraction. A soft ban restricts specific actions (writing reviews, joining events, placing bids, etc.) while letting the user continue browsing. A hard ban disables the Firebase Auth account entirely and cascades to suspend listings, cancel active bids, and revoke sessions. The support ticket system is built here because it is the primary channel through which bans get contested and resolved.
>
> **Soft ban model**: `UserDocument.softBans: UserSoftBan[]` â€” an array of scoped restrictions. Each entry has `action: BannedAction`, `reason: string`, `bannedBy: string` (employee uid), `bannedAt: Date`, `expiresAt?: Date` (null = permanent). Supported `BannedAction` values: `write_reviews`, `write_blog_comments`, `join_events`, `place_bids`, `create_listings`, `send_messages`, `create_support_tickets`, `report_scammers`. A user may have multiple simultaneous soft bans of different types.
>
> **Hard ban model**: `isDisabled: true` (already on `UserDocument`) + `hardBanReason?: string` + `hardBannedAt?: Date` + `hardBannedBy?: string`. Triggers Firebase Auth `updateUser(uid, { disabled: true })` via Admin SDK.
>
> **Support ticket rules** (enforced server-side, no client trust):
> - Max **2 active** (status: `open` | `in_progress` | `waiting_on_user`) general tickets per user at any time.
> - Order tickets: exactly **1 per non-completed order** (orders in status `PENDING`, `PROCESSING`, `SHIPPED`, `RETURN_REQUESTED` only â€” not `DELIVERED`, `CANCELLED`, `REFUNDED`).
> - Guests cannot create tickets â€” authentication required.
> - If user has `create_support_tickets` soft ban â†’ 403 "Your account is restricted from opening support tickets."
> - New ticket in same category not allowed while an existing one in that category is in `waiting_on_user` status (prevents spam reopening).
>
> **Notification routing (Firebase Functions)**: ticket events â†’ notify user + notify all employees who have `admin:support-tickets:read` permission. Ban events â†’ notify user + notify all employees with `admin:user-bans:read` permission. Notifications written to the `notifications` Firestore collection (existing schema) + Firebase Cloud Messaging push if device token present.
>
> **Do BAN1 â†’ BAN2 â†’ BAN3 â†’ BAN4 â†’ BAN5 â†’ BAN6 â†’ BAN7 â†’ BAN8 â†’ BAN9 in order.**

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
