## Tier SCAM â€” Scam Awareness System *(low priority)*

> **ًں“گ Layered shape (S14+):**
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/config.ts` â€” `SCAM_TYPES` (already exists; ensure exported from this path), `SCAM_CATEGORIES`, `SCAM_SEVERITY_LEVELS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/types.ts` â€” `ScamDocument`, `ScamProfile`, `ScamReport`, `ScamType`, `ScamCategory`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/schema.ts` â€” Zod for scam profile create/patch + report submission.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/scams/data.ts` â€” `getScamProfile(slug)` (React.cache), `listScams({ filters })`, `listSitemapScams()`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/scams/service.ts` â€” `assertScamRegisterAllowed(uid)`, `acknowledgeScamRegistration(uid)`; errors `ScamProfileNotFoundError`, `ScamReportRateLimitError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/scams/actions.ts` â€” `createScamProfile`, `updateScamProfile`, `submitScamReport`, `verifyScamReport` (`"use server"`; gated by RBAC `scam_moderator` / `trust_and_safety`).
> - **Repository:** existing `scammerRepository` (re-home reference under feature barrel).
> - **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/scamNotificationDispatch.ts` (notifies followers/community on new verified profile).
> - **Views:** `AdminScammersView`, `ScamProfilePublicView`, `ScamRegistrationAcknowledgementModal`, FAQ entries (content seed only â€” no view component).
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/scammers/page.tsx`, `[locale]/scams/[slug]/page.tsx`, `[locale]/scams/page.tsx` (list).
> - **OG + sitemap:** `src/app/[locale]/scams/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` (1200أ—630, profile card with masked identifier + scam type badges); `listSitemapScams()` exported and wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
> - **Error handling:** missing profile â†’ `notFound()`; admin-only mutate â†’ 403 with typed error code; report rate-limit â†’ toast.
> - **Verification:** SSR HTML for `/scams/<slug>` contains profile + JSON-LD `Person` markup; `curl -sI .../opengraph-image` â†’ 200 image/png; admin CRUD `tsc` 0/0; viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint.

> **Design intent**: A publicly visible, SEO-optimised scam database that (1) educates the collectibles community about how they get cheated, (2) names known bad actors with evidence, and (3) is mandatory reading for all new registrants. Admin employees verify and publish scammer profiles. The system is deeply integrated with the RBAC tier â€” only `scam_moderator` and `trust_and_safety` employees can verify profiles; any authenticated user can submit a report.
>
> **27 scam types** across 6 categories (defined as `SCAM_TYPES` constant in `appkit/src/features/scams/constants/scam-types.ts`):
>
> | Category | Types |
> |---|---|
> | **Price Manipulation** | `undervaluation` â€” tricks seller into believing item is worth far less ("it's just an old toy"); `fake_price_reference` â€” fake screenshot showing lower price elsewhere; `bait_and_switch` â€” advertises one price, changes after engagement; `condition_misrepresentation` â€” lists mint/sealed/graded, ships damaged/fake |
> | **Social Engineering** | `sympathy_play` â€” impersonates a student/child who "can't afford" market price, guilt-trips seller into discount or deferred payment; `trust_building_fraud` â€” months of small friendly purchases then one large scam; `urgency_pressure` â€” "I'm leaving the city in 1 hour, send now"; `student_impersonation` â€” specific variant: claims to be a broke student collector |
> | **Payment Fraud** | `advance_payment_ghost` â€” takes full advance payment then ghosts; `fake_payment_screenshot` â€” sends photoshopped UPI/PayTM success screenshot; `partial_payment_ghost` â€” pays earnest money, takes delivery, ghosts for rest; `chargeback_fraud` â€” pays via Razorpay/credit card, receives item, disputes with bank; `overpayment_scam` â€” "accidentally" overpays â‚¹5,000 for â‚¹500 item, asks for â‚¹4,500 refund before initial payment clears |
> | **Pre-order & Delivery Fraud** | `preorder_hold` â€” collects deposits from many buyers, holds money for months claiming "delays", eventually refunds only after public noise â€” never had a supplier; `fake_preorder_listing` â€” lists high-demand limited items for preorder with zero supplier relationship; `endless_delay_scam` â€” ships deliberately late (after refund window closes) with vague updates |
> | **Identity & Impersonation** | `seller_impersonation` â€” steals product photos from a reputable seller and runs identical listing at slightly lower price; `platform_impersonation` â€” fake "LetItRip Support" WhatsApp/DM asking for OTP/bank details; `account_takeover_resale` â€” hacks/takes over dormant legitimate seller account to exploit their review history; `fake_escrow` â€” creates a fake "middleman escrow" that is themselves |
> | **Item Authenticity Fraud** | `counterfeit_item` â€” sells replica/bootleg as genuine (fake holographic Pokأ©mon cards, recast Funko Pops, reproduction vintage Hot Wheels); `fake_grading_claim` â€” claims PSA/BGS graded, shows photoshopped certificate; `graded_case_tampering` â€” cracks a legitimate PSA slab, swaps in a fake/lower card, reseals; `sealed_product_repack` â€” opens booster boxes, removes valuable pulls, reseals with hot glue, resells as factory sealed |
> | **Logistics Fraud** | `empty_box_ship` â€” ships an empty box or rocks/newspaper; `fake_tracking_number` â€” generates tracking label but never drops package at courier; `return_swap_fraud` â€” receives genuine item, returns empty box or damaged swap, claims refund |
>
> **Scammer profile document** (`scammers` Firestore collection, prefix `scammer-`): `id`, `slug`, `displayName` (as they presented themselves), `phones: string[]`, `upiIds: string[]`, `emails: string[]`, `socialMedia: { platform: SocialPlatform; handle: string; url?: string }[]`, `scamType: ScamType`, `scamPlatform: ScamPlatform`, `description: string` (rich HTML â€” detailed account of what happened), `amountLost?: number` (paise), `itemInvolved?: string`, `evidence: string[]` (media URLs â€” chat screenshots, payment screenshots, listing photos), `reportedBy: string` (userId), `reportedByAnon: boolean` (if reporter chose to remain anonymous in public view), `status: "pending_review" \| "verified" \| "rejected" \| "removed"`, `verifiedBy?: string`, `verifiedAt?: Timestamp`, `relatedScammerIds: string[]`, `tags: string[]`, `seoSlug: string`, `views: number`, `createdAt: Timestamp`, `updatedAt: Timestamp`. **`ScamPlatform`**: `"letitrip" \| "whatsapp" \| "olx" \| "facebook_marketplace" \| "instagram_dms" \| "telegram" \| "in_person" \| "local_market" \| "other"`. **`SocialPlatform`**: `"instagram" \| "facebook" \| "twitter_x" \| "whatsapp" \| "telegram" \| "youtube" \| "other"`.
>
> **SEO-first design**: every scammer profile page has a unique `/scams/[slug]` route, full `generateMetadata` (name in title, scam type in description, og:image from evidence), FAQ schema JSON-LD, and phone/UPI/email plaintext in the HTML so they are indexed by search engines. The goal: someone searching a phone number or UPI ID finds our page immediately.
>
> **Mandatory registration acknowledgement**: after email verification, new users see a non-skippable scam awareness modal with 5 key facts (one per scam category), a link to `/scams`, and a required checkbox "I have read the scam awareness guide and understand these risks." Tracked as `scamAwarenessAcknowledgedAt?: Timestamp` on `UserDocument`. The modal is shown until acknowledged; after acknowledgement it never appears again.
>
> **Do SCAM1 â†’ SCAM2 â†’ SCAM3 â†’ SCAM4 â†’ SCAM5 â†’ SCAM6 â†’ SCAM7 â†’ SCAM8 in order. SCAM9 (RBAC wiring) should be done alongside RBAC4/RBAC7 when that tier is implemented.**

## Tier AX â€” Action System & URL Patterns

> **Design intent**: (1) Eliminate ~200 copy-pasted onClick router.push + toast chains across admin/store/public pages via a typed ACTION constant system with useActionDispatch() hook. (2) Make every admin/store CRUD panel deep-linkable via URL search params (?panel=create / ?panel=edit&id=slug). (3) Standardise sticky form action bars across all FormShell-based forms.
>
> **Implementation order**: AX1 -> AX2 (depends on AX1) -> AX3 (depends on UX1 FormShell).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| AX1 | Centralized ACTION constants + useActionDispatch hook | M | âœ… | **Session 90 (2026-05-11) â€” fully done.** Constants: `appkit/src/features/products/constants/action-defs.ts` â€” ACTION_ID/ROW_ACTION_ID/FORM_ACTION_ID/DASHBOARD_QUICK_ACTION_ID + all META maps + preset groups. Hook: `appkit/src/react/hooks/use-action-dispatch.ts` â€” useActionDispatch(options?) returns async dispatch(action) handling NAVIGATE/OPEN_PANEL/TOAST/BULK/COPY. Store: `appkit/src/stores/panel-store.ts` â€” Zustand usePanelStore (panelId, data, openPanel, closePanel, isPanelOpen). Zustand v5 added to appkit deps. Migration: SellerProductsView.tsx handleEdit migrated from router.push to dispatch({ type: "NAVIGATE" }). All exported from client.ts + index.ts. 0 TS errors both repos, appkit build clean. |
| AX2 | Edit/Create URL routing â€” panel auto-open on URL params | M | âœ… | **Session 92 (2026-05-11) â€” done.** usePanelUrlSync hook (URL ?panel=create/edit&id=xxx); DataTable onRowClick prop; embedded prop on all 7 AdminXxxEditorViews; 8 admin listing views wired with inline SideDrawer + embedded editor; exported from index.ts + client.ts. 0 TS errors both repos. | Depends on AX1. **Pattern**: listing pages read URL search params ?panel=create or ?panel=edit&id={slug}. On mount: if params present -> dispatch(ACTION.OPEN_PANEL(panelId, { id })). On panel onClose/onSuccess -> router.replace(basePath) (removes query params). **usePanelUrlSync(panelId, basePath)** hook (new, appkit/src/hooks/): reads useSearchParams(), on mount calls dispatch if params match, subscribes to panelStore â€” when panel closes, calls router.replace(basePath). **Deep-link format**: /admin/products?panel=create (create panel opens); /admin/products?panel=edit&id=product-abc (edit panel opens pre-loaded). **Wire into**: admin products, auctions, preorders, stores, categories, brands, blog, events, FAQs, coupons (10 admin listing pages) + all store-seller listing pages. **Share**: copy icon in panel header -> ACTION.COPY(window.location.href, "Edit link copied") after URL is updated on open. Add ROUTES.ADMIN.PRODUCT_EDIT(id) etc. helper functions to route-map. npx tsc --noEmit -> 0 errors. |

## Tier FI â€” Product Feature Icons & Badges

> **Design intent**: A flexible feature-flagging system for listings. Platform defines standard icons (free shipping, verified seller, condition badges, etc.). Stores and admin can create custom feature icons. Products carry a features: string[] array of feature IDs. Cards and detail pages render small icon badges. Some features are product-type specific (e.g., Auction Winner Badge applies to auctions only). Slug prefix: feature-.

## Tier BK â€” Public Bulk Actions

> **Design intent**: Let both authenticated and guest users select multiple products on listing pages and perform bulk actions (compare, wishlist, share). Selection state is ephemeral (in-memory only, not persisted). Guest users can compare and share; auth users additionally add to wishlist. Compare is capped at 4 items. The compare overlay shows items side-by-side (desktop: table; mobile: swipeable cards).

## Tier WA â€” WhatsApp Business Integration *(low priority â€” post-alpha)*

> **ًں“گ Layered shape (S14+ remaining tasks):** WA1â€“WA4 are âœ… in legacy paths; any new WA work and any WA migration to the new layout follows this shape:

> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/whatsapp/data.ts` â€” `getWaConfigForStore(storeId)` (decrypted token never leaves server).
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/whatsapp/service.ts` â€” `assertWaCapability(storeId)` (RBAC `whatsapp_catalog_sync`); errors `WaCapabilityMissingError`, `WaCatalogSyncError`.

> **Design intent**: Allow store owners to sync their standard products to their own WhatsApp Business Catalog (per-store Meta credentials). Platform admin receives a WhatsApp message (Meta Cloud API) whenever a new order is placed â€” announcement also sent to the store owner. Group posting is not possible via API; a wa.me share link is provided instead. Full plan in `C:\Users\mohsi\.claude\plans\plan-and-add-support-compressed-snowflake.md`.

> The GD task rows below remain as the **authoritative content-source spec** for the corresponding DX MDX pages â€” port the section content verbatim. Do not mark GD rows âœ… when implementing DX; track progress on DX rows instead. Three pieces remain in-app because they depend on live user state: DX32 (capability gates), DX33 (personalized onboarding checklist), DX34 (sidebar Help links + footer links).
>
> ~~Original spec preserved below for content reference:~~

> **ًں“گ Layered shape (S14+):** pure RSC content â€” no Firestore reads, no mutations.
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/guides/config.ts` â€” `GUIDE_SLUGS`, `GUIDE_CATEGORIES`, `GUIDE_AUDIENCES` (admin / store / buyer).
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/guides/types.ts` â€” `GuideEntry`, `GuideCategory`, `GuideSection`.
> - **Validation:** **N/A** (static content).
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/guides/data.ts` â€” `listGuides({ audience })`, `getGuide(slug)`, `listSitemapGuides()` (all read static module â€” no Firestore).
> - **Business logic:** **N/A** (read-only).
> - **Actions:** **N/A**.
> - **Repository:** **N/A** â€” content lives at `_internal/shared/features/guides/content/<slug>.mdx` (or `.tsx` if richer).
> - **Orchestration:** **N/A**.
> - **Views:** `GuideHubView`, `GuidePageView`, `GuideSidebar` (audience-scoped TOC).
> - **Consumer wiring:** `src/app/[locale]/help/page.tsx` (buyer hub), `src/app/[locale]/help/<slug>/page.tsx`; `src/app/[locale]/admin/guide/<slug>/page.tsx`; `src/app/[locale]/store/guide/<slug>/page.tsx` â€” all pure RSC, capability/permission filtered for admin/store hubs.
> - **OG + sitemap:** per-guide `src/app/[locale]/help/<slug>/opengraph-image.tsx` (1200أ—630, audience badge + title); `listSitemapGuides()` exported and wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
> - **Error handling:** missing slug â†’ `notFound()`; admin guide accessed without permission â†’ render skeleton with "You don't have access to this guide" notice (do NOT 403, since the index entry should still render).
> - **Verification:** Lighthouse SEO â‰¥ 95 per guide; viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint; `tsc` 0/0; `npm run build` succeeds with all new RSC pages compiled.

> **Design intent**: Rich, section-based guide pages embedded in all three dashboards (admin, store, buyer) and the public help center. Unlike the FAQ system (short Q&A answers), guides are long-form reference documents with step-by-step walkthroughs, field-by-field form explanations, status lifecycle diagrams, capability/permission upgrade prompts, and plain-language summaries written for non-technical users. Goal: any user â€” seller, buyer, or internal employee â€” should be able to understand every feature, form, and workflow without leaving the app.
>
> **Three guide surfaces**: (1) **Admin guide** â€” lives at `/admin/guide/*`, accessible to all admin and employee roles; permission-aware (only shows sections the logged-in employee can access). Covers every admin panel and all 18 employee permission groups. (2) **Store guide** â€” lives inside `/store/guide/*`, accessible only to store owners. Covers every seller-facing feature and all 18 store capabilities. (3) **Buyer help center** â€” lives at public `/help/*`, accessible without login. Covers the complete buyer journey.
>
> **Sidebar placement (enforced for all three)**: every guide hub must have a dedicated nav entry in its dashboard sidebar â€” admin: `ADMIN_NAV_GROUPS` Help group (bottom of sidebar); store: `STORE_NAV_GROUPS` Help group; user dashboard: `USER_NAV_GROUPS` Help link pointing to public `/help`. Sidebar entries are wired in GD13 for admin; GD1 already covers store; GD7 covers the user/footer links.
>
> **Content rules**: use only appkit primitives (`Section`, `Container`, `Heading`, `Text`, `Badge`, `Alert`, `Collapsible`, `Stack`, `Row`). No hardcoded hex or breakpoints. All guide content is static (no Firestore reads) â€” these are pre-authored pages, not CMS-driven. Brand name **LetItRip** throughout. Collectibles-niche examples only (Pokأ©mon TCG, Hot Wheels, Beyblades, anime figures).
>
> **Sequence**: GD1â€“GD6 (store guides) and GD7â€“GD11 (buyer guides) are independent. GD12 depends on RBAC8. GD13â€“GD22 (admin guides) depend on RBAC1 for permission-aware rendering but can be built as static pages first and made permission-aware in the same session as RBAC3/RBAC7.

`background.type` (image/video/color/gradient); `cards[]` array inside each slide; how to reorder slides (drag in AdminCarouselView); why you cannot have 2 slides of the same `background.type: "video"` active at once (performance constraint). **Section 5 â€” Homepage sections**: 21 section types; `order` field drives render sequence; `enabled: false` hides without deleting; config shape varies per type â€” always refer to `appkit/src/features/homepage/schemas/firestore.ts` for the authoritative shape; never manually edit Firestore documents â€” always use AdminSectionsView. **Section 6 â€” Ads**: ad slot keys and where they render on the page; `isActive` vs `startDate`/`endDate` scheduling; `impressions` + `clicks` counters are read-only. **Section 7 â€” Newsletter**: how subscribers are stored; export flow; legal note (CAN-SPAM / Indian IT Act â€” unsubscribe must be honoured). `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |
| GD19 | Admin: Site Configuration Guide | S | âڈ³ | **New page** `/admin/guide/site`. **New view** `AdminSiteConfigGuideView`. Requires `admin:site:read` or full admin. **Section 1 â€” Site Settings overview**: the 12 setting groups (branding, appearance, announcementBanner, seoDefaults, contactSocial, watermark, fees, integrations, shipping, auctionConfig, platformLimits, legalPages); singleton document at `site_settings/global` â€” only one exists; never delete this document. **Section 2 â€” Integrations (API keys)**: which keys are stored here (Razorpay, Firebase, Shiprocket, WhatsApp, SendGrid, Google Analytics, etc.); keys are write-only in the UI (shown as "â€¢â€¢â€¢â€¢â€¢â€¢" after saving); how to rotate a key (enter new value, save â€” old value is immediately replaced); warn: deleting the value from the UI does NOT rotate the key at the provider â€” revoke it there first. **Section 3 â€” Platform limits**: `maxOpenTicketsPerUser` (default 2); `maxOrderTicketsPerOrder` (default 1); `maxImagesPerProduct`; `minBidIncrementPaise`; `auctionConfig.defaultExtensionMinutes`; `auctionConfig.paymentWindowHours` â€” changing these mid-operation affects all in-flight auctions and tickets, so change with care. **Section 4 â€” Navigation editor**: `nav-` prefix for nav items; adding a nav item to `MAIN_NAV_ITEMS` in admin makes it appear in the public top bar; `isExternal: true` for external links (opens in new tab); never delete a nav item that is referenced in marketing materials without replacing the URL. **Section 5 â€” Feature flags**: what feature flags control (experimental features, A/B tests); how to roll out (set flag â†’ test in staging â†’ set for all). `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |

Groups: `content_moderator` (moderates reviews + comments), `review_manager` (reviews + products:read), `blog_poster` (blog:read/write/publish), `community_manager` (events + newsletter + contact), `event_handler` (events read/write/delete + entries), `newsletter_manager` (newsletter + contact), `seo_manager` (site:read + faqs + blog:read + analytics:view), `ad_manager` (ads + featured + deals), `site_manager` (site:read/write + navigation + sections + carousel + ads + feature-flags), `catalog_manager` (products + categories + brands + reviews:read + media), `finance_manager` (payouts + orders:read + analytics:view), `data_analyst` (analytics:view + orders:read + users:read + carts:read + wishlists:read), `customer_support` (support-tickets:read/write/assign/close + orders:read/write + returns:read/write + users:read + contact:read + notifications:read/write), `store_onboarding` (stores:read/write + store-addresses:read + brands:read + categories:read + users:read), `trust_and_safety` (user-bans:read/write + support-tickets all + scammers:read/write/verify + users:read + media:read/write), `auction_monitor` (bids:read/write + products:read + orders:read + users:read), `scam_moderator` (scammers:read/write/verify/delete + users:read + media:read/write), `support_agent` (dashboard:view + support-tickets:read/write/assign/close + orders:read/write + returns:read/write + users:read + contact:read + notifications:read/write). **Section 3 â€” Inviting an employee**: step-by-step (Admin Team page â†’ Invite Employee â†’ enter email + select group â†’ system sends invite email with temp password â†’ employee logs in â†’ forced password change). **Section 4 â€” Customising permissions** ("Custom" group): when to deviate from a preset; the domain tabs in the editor (Management / Finance / Catalog / Content / Site / Events); System tab intentionally omitted from employee permission picker (sessions, feature-flags, copilot, team are admin-only). **Section 5 â€” Revoking access**: what "Revoke access" does (sets `isDisabled: true` + clears `permissions` â€” does NOT delete user doc for audit trail); why revoking is preferable to deleting; how to re-enable (set `isDisabled: false` + re-assign permissions). **Section 6 â€” Permission audit best practices**: review employee permissions quarterly; log of who granted what is stored in `users/{uid}/banHistory` subcollection (reused for permission change events). `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |
| GD21 | Admin: Analytics Guide | S | âڈ³ | **New page** `/admin/guide/analytics`. **New view** `AdminAnalyticsGuideView`. | GD22 | Admin: Trust & Safety Guide â€” bans, scams, support tickets | L | âڈ³ | **New page** `/admin/guide/trust`. **New view** `AdminTrustGuideView`. hard ban = disables Firebase Auth account, suspends store, cancels bids, revokes sessions â€” nuclear option; when to use each (soft ban: single policy violation; hard ban: fraud, persistent abuse, legal requirement). **Section 2 â€” Applying a soft ban** (step-by-step): open Admin Users â†’ find user â†’ Moderation tab â†’ Add soft ban â†’ select action + reason + optional expiry â†’ Save; user receives notification immediately; ban is enforced server-side on the relevant API route; expired bans are treated as lifted without deletion. **Section 3 â€” Applying a hard ban** (step-by-step + cascade effects): Moderation tab â†’ "Suspend account" toggle â†’ enter reason â†’ Confirm; cascade: Auth disabled â†’ sessions deleted â†’ store suspended â†’ active bids cancelled â†’ notification sent to user; how to lift (Unban button â€” does NOT auto-restore listings). **Section 4 â€” Ban appeal process**: user contacts support via email (not ticket â€” `create_support_tickets` is soft-banned); `trust_and_safety` employee reviews evidence; lift via Admin Users â†’ Moderation tab. **Section 5 â€” Scam report workflow** (for `scam_moderator` and `trust_and_safety`): report comes in with `status: "pending_review"`; admin reviews identity + evidence + incident description; "Verify & Publish" (sets `status: "verified"`, notifies reporter) vs "Reject" (notifies reporter with reason); editing a verified profile (updating fields does NOT reset status); contest handling â€” if accused contests, review `contests` subcollection â†’ "Uphold" (update profile + mark contest resolved) vs "Dismiss"; when to "Remove" a verified profile (false identity, legal takedown). **Section 6 â€” Support ticket workflow** (for `customer_support` and `support_agent`): ticket states (open â†’ in_progress â†’ waiting_on_user â†’ resolved â†’ closed); who can do what (read: all support roles; write/reply: read/write; assign: assign permission; close: close permission); SLA guidelines (first response within 4 hours for high/urgent; 24 hours for normal; 48 hours for low); escalation path (escalate priority + notify all `admin:support-tickets:read` employees); internal notes field (never visible to user â€” use for escalation context, account observations). **Section 7 â€” Trust metrics** (`Alert variant="info"`): how `helpfulCount` on reviews works; how `views` on scammer profiles is used (trending scam types); how to interpret `reportedByAnon` (reporter chose anonymity â€” do not expose their identity even internally). `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |

## Sessions SB1â€“SB10 â€” Bundle & Prize Draw Listings + Event Raffle System
> Added: 2026-05-11

> **ًں“گ Layered shape (mandatory for every SB row):** every SB-series task above the `Status` column must, when implemented, conform to the shape below. Existing single-line `Notes` columns predate the SSR rearch and stay as-is for reference; the layered breakdown below is the **authoritative spec** for implementation.
>
> **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/config.ts` â€” `BUNDLE_MAX_ITEMS`, `BUNDLE_MAX_PER_USER_DEFAULT`, `PRIZE_DRAW_MIN_ITEMS`, `PRIZE_DRAW_MAX_ITEMS`, `PRIZE_DRAW_REVEAL_DEADLINE_DAYS_DEFAULT`, `EVENT_RAFFLE_TYPES`, `SPIN_PRIZE_MAX`.
>
> **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/types.ts` â€” `BundleDocument`, `BundleItem`, `PrizeDrawDocument`, `PrizeDrawItem`, `EventRaffleConfig`, `SpinPrize`, `ListingType` (extended union: `"standard" | "auction" | "pre-order" | "prize-draw" | "bundle"`).
>
> **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/schema.ts` â€” Zod discriminated union on `listingType`; `prizeDrawItemSchema` (min 3, max 16); `bundleItemSchema` (min 2 child products); `spinPrizeSchema` (weighted; sum of weights normalised server-side).
>
> **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/data.ts` â€” `getBundle(slug)`, `listBundles({ filters, page, pageSize })`, `getPrizeDraw(slug)`, `listPrizeDraws()`, `getEventRaffle(eventId)`, `listSitemapBundles()`, `listSitemapPrizeDraws()`, `listSitemapEventRaffles()`. All reads use `React.cache`.
>
> **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/service.ts` â€” `assertBundleStock(bundleId, qty)`, `assertBundlePerUserLimit(uid, bundleId)`, `assertPrizeDrawNotExpired(drawId)`, `assertPrizeDrawCapacity(drawId)`, `assertRafflePoolNonEmpty(eventId)`, `assertSpinNotUsed(uid, eventId)`. Domain errors: `BundleStockError`, `BundleNonRefundableConsentMissingError`, `BundlePerUserLimitError`, `PrizeDrawExpiredError`, `PrizeDrawCapacityError`, `RafflePoolExhaustedError`, `SpinAlreadyUsedError`.
>
> **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/actions.ts` â€” `createBundle`, `updateBundle`, `deleteBundle`, `purchaseBundle`, `revealPrize`, `triggerEventRaffle`, `assignSpinPrize` (`"use server"`).
>
> **Repository:** new `bundlesRepository`, `prizeDrawsRepository`, `eventRafflesRepository` in `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts` â€” extending `BaseRepository` (override `createWithId` per recurrent root-cause #9). Migration script for `listingType` discriminator move (SB1-A) replaces the legacy `isAuction`/`isPreOrder` boolean pair across all collections.
>
> **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/{onBundlePurchase,prizeDrawAutoRefund,prizeDrawReveal,eventRaffleSpin,eventRaffleWinnerNotify,bundleStockSync}.ts` â€” registered via `bindToFirebase()` per Arch-S6.
>
> **Views:** `_internal/client/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/<X>View.tsx` â€” `BundleDetailView`, `BundlesListView`, `BundleItemsPicker`, `BundleForm`, `NonRefundableConsentModal`, `PrizeDrawDetailView`, `PrizeDrawItemsEditor`, `PrizeRevealModal`, `Collage`, `EventRaffleWinnerView`, `SpinWheelView`.
>
> **Consumer wiring:** `src/app/[locale]/bundles/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/bundles/[slug]/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/[slug]/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/events/[slug]/winner/page.tsx`, plus store/admin sub-pages â€” every page pre-fetches via the data fn and passes `initialBundle` / `initialPrizeDraw` / `initialEventRaffle`.
>
> **OG + sitemap:** `src/app/[locale]/bundles/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/events/[slug]/winner/opengraph-image.tsx`. Sitemap data fns wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
>
> **Error handling:** stock-out â†’ inline form error + cart-line removal; expired prize draw â†’ 410 page; raffle pool empty â†’ admin notification + buyer 404; non-refundable consent missing â†’ checkout-blocking modal; per-user limit exceeded â†’ toast + `Add to wishlist` CTA.
>
> **Verification:** SSR HTML for bundle/prize-draw/raffle detail contains title + price + items; `auto-refund` job dry-run; `crypto.randomInt`-based reveal/spin reproducible only with stored seed; viewport sweep xs â†’ 2xl + dark-mode repaint on every new page; `tsc` 0/0; `audit-violations` exit 0.

| SB4-H | Prize Reveal API route â€” crypto.randomInt + pool exhaustion | âœ… | **Done S7-PrizeDraws-prep3 2026-05-13.** New `src/app/api/prize-draws/[id]/reveal/route.ts`. POST body `{ orderId }`; auth required. Pre-tx existence + ownership + payment + window + deadline checks (fail-fast). Transactional reveal: re-reads product + order under lock, re-checks idempotency, filters `unwonItems`, picks via `crypto.randomInt(0, unwonItems.length)`, flips `items[pickIndex].isWon = true` on the product doc, writes `order.prizeWon`. Pool-exhausted path marks the order REFUNDED + `isNonRefundable: false` + returns `{ refunded: true, reason: "pool_exhausted" }` (covers SB8-C). Idempotent: re-posting after success returns the same prize without re-rolling. Public response never echoes the prize pool's `isWon` map. ~~Original spec:~~ **New file:** `src/app/api/prize-draws/[id]/reveal/route.ts`. POST `{ orderId }`. Auth required. Steps: verify order ownership + paid; verify `order.prizeDrawProductId === productId`; idempotency check (`order.prizeWon === null`); verify `prizeRevealStatus === "open"` + within window + before deadline; filter `unwonItems`; if empty â†’ refund + return `{ refunded: true, reason: "pool_exhausted" }`; else `crypto.randomInt(0, unwonItems.length)` â†’ pick winner; update order.prizeWon; set prizeDrawItem.isWon=true; return `{ prizeWon: { itemNumber, title, images, estimatedValue } }`. `npx tsc --noEmit` â†’ 0 errors. |

On "Reveal my prize" CTA it calls `/api/prize-draws/[id]/reveal` (or a `onReveal` slot for custom envs), then runs a 3.2-second decelerating highlight cycle (`CYCLE_INTERVAL_FAST` 80 ms â†’ `CYCLE_INTERVAL_SLOW` 360 ms) across the collage using `highlightItemNumber`, finally landing on the winning tile. After animation: winner card with image + estimated value. Pool-exhausted + already-revealed branches handled. ### SB11 â€” Homepage Sections: Bundles, Prize Draws & Event Raffles

> **Why here:** Bundles and prize draws are new listing types (SB1â€“SB4). They need dedicated homepage section types so the CMS admin can surface them on the homepage â€” the same way standard products, auctions, and pre-orders already have section types. Event raffles (SB9) also get a section type so live raffle events can be promoted on the homepage. All three section types are **additive** â€” no existing section types change. Seed docs are disabled-by-default so they don't render before the underlying data exists. SB11 depends on the schemas from SB1-A (listingType), SB1-E (BundleDocument), SB4 (PrizeDrawDocument shape), and SB9-A/SB9-B (EventType raffle). SB11 can be planned and scaffolded independently; it needs SB3/SB4/SB9 data to actually render anything.
>
> **Relationship to SB5-D:** SB5-D planned seeding `section-featured-bundles` and `section-prize-draws` as "reuse existing section types". Those types don't exist yet. SB11-A defines them. SB11-G handles the three new disabled seed docs. SB5-D should be updated to only seed `section-brand-hot-wheels` and `section-brand-pokemon` (which reuse existing `brand-spotlight` or `brands` section types).
>
> **Session assignment:** SB11 fits into Session 93 alongside EX1â€“EX5/YT1 (extended homepage sections). All three new section components are async RSC and query their own collections â€” no architecture change needed.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| SB11-A | Schema â€” 3 new HomepageSectionType values + config interfaces | M | âœ… | S7 2026-05-11. `"featured-bundles" \| "prize-draws" \| "event-raffles"` added to `SectionType` union. `FeaturedBundlesSectionConfig`, `PrizeDrawsSectionConfig`, `EventRafflesSectionConfig` interfaces added. `SectionConfig` discriminated union extended. `DEFAULT_SECTION_ORDER` updated (20/21/22). 0 TSC errors. |

## Tier LR â€” Lint Refactor: Raw HTML Element Migration *(stamped 2026-05-12)*

> Added 2026-05-12. `lir/no-raw-html-elements` + `lir/no-raw-media-elements` errored across 36 legacy files (192 errors total) blocking the `npm run check` gate. Each file got a top-of-file `/* eslint-disable lir/no-raw-html-elements, lir/no-raw-media-elements -- LR1: legacy raw HTML, migration tracked in crud-tracker.md Tier LR */` stamp so the gate exits 0 without losing the migration backlog. **Every disabled file is a row in this tier â€” closing a row removes the disable.**
>
> **Migration recipe per file:** (1) replace `<h1>`/`<h2>`/`<h3>` with `<Heading level={N}>`; `<p>` with `<Text>`; `<span>` with `<Span>` or `<Text inline>`; `<button>` with `<Button variant=â€¦>`; `<a>` with `<TextLink>` or `<Link>` (from `@/i18n/navigation`); `<img>` with `<Image>` (next/image) or `<MediaImage>`; `<video>` with `<MediaVideo>`. (2) Remove the file-top disable. (3) Run `npm run check:lint -- <file>` to confirm zero errors. (4) Re-flow the file through `npm run check` end-to-end.

|---|------|-------------|--------|-------|
| LR1-01 | `src/components/dev/SeedPanel.tsx` | 26 | âڈ³ | Dev tooling; heavy raw `<div>`/`<span>` use. Big file (>1200 LOC) â€” split the migration into Basics / Accordion / per-collection card sections. |
| LR1-02 | `src/app/[locale]/scams/report/page.tsx` | 23 | âڈ³ | Form-heavy. Replace each native `<input>`/`<label>`/`<button>` pair with appkit `<Input>` + `<Label>` + `<Button>`. Co-ordinate with SCAM2 form polish session if it lands first. |

### LR2 â€” Appkit lint backlog *(separate from letitrip src)*

> Discovered 2026-05-12. `npm run check`'s `check:lint` step only lints `src/**` (letitrip). Running `npx eslint src/**/*.{ts,tsx}` inside `appkit/` surfaces **404 errors** that the gate doesn't see today. Adding appkit lint to the gate now would block all forward work; this row tracks the cleanup so it gets done.

| # | Rule | Count | Status | Migration approach |
|---|------|-------|--------|--------------------|
| LR2-A | `@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any` | 228 | âڈ³ | Each `any` is a type-debt entry. Sweep by feature (e.g. `appkit/src/features/products/**`, then `auctions/**`). Per file: replace with concrete type, `unknown`, or generic. Some inevitable in adapter layers â€” leave `// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any` with a `LR2-A: <reason>` comment. |
| LR2-B | `@typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars` | 150 | âڈ³ | Mostly unused params + leftover imports from refactors. `--fix` handles many; the rest are intentional (destructured `_ignored`) and need `_` prefix. |
| LR2-C | `@typescript-eslint/no-empty-object-type` | 21 | âڈ³ | `interface Foo {}` placeholders left over from incremental design. Either give them a body or replace with `type Foo = Record<string, never>`. |
| LR2-D | Other (`prefer-const`, malformed JSDoc) | 5 | âڈ³ | One-off cleanups. |

**Activation plan**: once LR2-A/B/C land, wire appkit eslint into the root `npm run check:lint` so future regressions block the gate.

## Tier OG â€” OpenGraph Image Coverage *(post-alpha; backlog audit)*

> **Design intent:** every public detail page (one resource at one URL) ships an `opengraph-image.tsx` so social shares render rich previews. As of 2026-05-12, 7 detail families have OG images (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores, brands, blog, events). This tier closes the gap on existing routes; OG tasks for **new** resources (bundles, prize-draws, scams, guides, etc.) live with their own tier and are not duplicated here.
>
> **ًں“گ Layered shape (S14+):** OG tasks are pure consumer-wiring + verification â€” most layers **N/A**. *Data layer*: reuse the existing per-feature `data.ts` getter (`getCategoryBySlug`, `faqRepository.getBySlug`, etc.). *Consumer wiring*: the new `opengraph-image.tsx` file itself, edge runtime, `ImageResponse` 1200أ—630. *OG + sitemap*: this row IS the OG task; sitemap entries already exist on the listing data fns. *Error handling*: missing resource â†’ fall back to default OG image at `src/app/opengraph-image.tsx`. *Verification*: `curl -sI http://localhost:3000/<route>/opengraph-image` â†’ `200 image/png` + visual check in Twitter/Facebook debugger; `npm run build` includes the new edge route.

|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| OG1 | OG image for category detail page | S | âœ… | **Done S6 2026-05-13.** `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/categories/og.tsx` â€” two-layer renderer (`renderCategoryOg` mapping CategoryDocument â†’ OG data; `renderCategoryOgImage` pure JSX primitive) â€” cover image background from `display.coverImage`, name + 140-char description + product-count chip from `metrics.totalItemCount`. `src/app/[locale]/categories/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` thin page shim. Node runtime per OG-FIX1. Pagination wrappers (`categories/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]`, `categories/[slug]/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]`) are exempt in `verify-og-coverage.mjs` â€” OG belongs on the canonical detail. |

| OG-FIX1 | Edge-runtime build break â€” `node:fs` / `crypto` in OG routes | M | âœ… S23-follow-up 2026-05-12 â€” applied fix path (a): dropped `export const runtime = "edge"` from all 9 OG routes via the new `scripts/strip-og-edge.mjs` helper. Original notes: | **Production blocker.** Verified S23 2026-05-12: `npm run build` fails at `Collecting page data` with `Failed to load external module node:fs: Native module not found: node:fs` originating from `/[locale]/blog/[slug]/opengraph-image` (and likely all sibling edge OG routes). Root cause: OG routes declare `runtime = "edge"` but import from `@mohasinac/appkit/server`, whose chain pulls in `appkit/dist/features/auth/token-store.js` (`import crypto from "crypto"`) and `consent-otp.js` (`import { createHmac, randomInt } from "crypto"`). | OG-FIX2 | `outputFileTracingIncludes` moved out of `experimental` | XS | âœ… S23-follow-up 2026-05-12 â€” `appkit/src/configs/next.ts` `defineNextConfig` now reads `outputFileTracingIncludes` as a top-level override key, merges the firebase-admin/lib/database forcing as the default, and emits it at the top of the returned config (not under `experimental`). `NextConfigOverride` interface gained the typed field. `npm run build` no longer prints the "Unrecognized key" warning. | DEV-1 | `watch:css` produces degraded `dist/tailwind-utilities.css` | S | âڈ³ | Discovered S23 2026-05-12 via the Stop hook: when `npm run dev` is left running, appkit's `watch:css` overwrites `dist/tailwind-utilities.css` with a build missing the `md:` / `lg:` breakpoint utilities (Tailwind scans `dist/` before TSC has finished emitting, so the `min-width:768px` / `min-width:1024px` class strings aren't seen and get purged). `verify-css-build` then fails on next `npm run check`. One-command recovery: `npm --prefix ./appkit run build`. **Fix paths**: (a) point `watch:css` at `src/**` (not `dist/**`), (b) gate `watch:css` on a first-pass TSC completion via a small wrapper, or (c) restore the build CSS on dev shutdown via the `killTree` hook in `scripts/dev-next.mjs`. Tracked so the next audit failure has a one-link explanation. |
| DEV-2 | Dev heap cap probe: 1024 MB OOMs, 2048 MB stable | S | âœ… S23-followup 2026-05-12 â€” new `scripts/probe-dev-heap-cap.mjs` boots `next dev --webpack` at incremental caps (1024 â†’ 1536 â†’ 2048 â€¦) with light load (6 routes rotated every 4 s for 2 min/cap), distinguishing natural OOM from deliberate-kill. Results on this codebase: 1024 MB OOMs (peak RSS 1457 MB), 1536 MB survives (peak RSS 1887 MB), 2048 MB over-permissive (V8 grows to fill). Per "minimum no-crash + 512 MB headroom" rule â†’ **2048 MB**. Applied to `package.json` `dev:only` NODE_OPTIONS, `scripts/dev-next.mjs` HOBBY_LIMITS.MEMORY_MB, `scripts/next-memory-forensics.js` HEAP_CAP_MB default. CLAUDE.md Rule #6 + `memory/project_vercel_hobby_limits.md` rewritten for Fluid Compute Standard reality (2 GB per-function, 8 GB build machine). |
| DEV-3 | Vercel `.next/` upload OOM blocked deploy | XS | âœ… S23-followup 2026-05-12 â€” first `vercel --prod` attempt blew up the CLI with `Array buffer allocation failed` because 41 GB of `.next/` build cache + leaked heap snapshots sat in the upload tree. `.vercelignore` now excludes `.next/`, `memory-forensics-*`, `*.heapsnapshot`, `probe-results.json`. Subsequent upload was 2.2 MB. |
| DEV-4 | Vercel build broken on `firebase-functions/v2/*` (Module not found) | M | âœ… S23-followup 2026-05-12 â€” appkit's `server-entry.ts` re-exported `bindToFirebase` + 22 job handlers from `_internal/server/jobs/index`, which imports `firebase-functions/v2/{https,scheduler,firestore}`. Local webpack dev externalised those via `defineNextConfig`'s `externals` callback; **Vercel's prod build uses Turbopack** which won't externalize an uninstalled package. Two failed published versions chased this (2.5.0 had the issue; 2.5.1 added `firebase-functions` to `FIREBASE_EXTERNAL_PACKAGES` but Turbopack ignored it). **Fix: carved `@mohasinac/appkit/jobs` subpath** in 2.6.0 â€” bindToFirebase + handler re-exports moved there, server-entry.ts dropped the block. `functions/src/index.ts` updated to import from `@mohasinac/appkit/jobs`. Letitrip's Next bundle never reaches `firebase-functions` now. |
| DEV-5 | Prod deploy live on `www.letitrip.in` | XS | âœ… S23-followup 2026-05-12 â€” after DEV-3 + DEV-4 fixes, `vercel deploy --prod --yes` succeeded. Deployment `letitrip-pmnjd95r1-mohasin-ahamed-chinnapattans-projects.vercel.app` aliased to `https://www.letitrip.in`; `curl -sI` returns `HTTP/1.1 200 OK` + Next 16 font + CSS preload chain. SB3 (Bundle Listings) + all S23 work is now in production. |

## Tier EMG â€” Emerging Patterns *(holding bay for code/copy mentions without tasks)*

> **Process note:** whenever a session notices a feature, payment method, integration, or content type that is referenced in code or copy but has no implementation task, **append a row here in the same session â€” do not wait for triage**. EMG is the holding bay until a feature graduates into its own tier or scheduled session. Re-scan triggers: any new mention surfaced by `grep` for keywords (`EMI`, `installment`, `gift card`, `loyalty`, `live chat`, `affiliate`, `referral`, `crypto`, `subscription`, `B2B`, `wholesale`); any FAQ or seed-copy mention of a flow with no code path; any partial implementation in `letitrip.in/functions/src/` not surfaced in the public app. Each row carries the full layered shape (or explicit **N/A**) so it is implementation-ready when scheduled.

## Tier RA â€” Retrofit Audit (SSR-Design Conformance) *(audits âœ… tasks against the layered template)*

> One audit row per existing tier that has âœ… rows. Each audit walks the tier and confirms each feature against the SSR-design checklist below. Audit rows are **read-only**; any gap flips the original âœ… to âڑ ï¸ڈ and adds a concrete fix row under the original tier (one commit = one work unit).
>
> **Checklist applied per feature:**
> ```
> â–، TEMPLATE     _internal/server/features/<feature>/ has data.ts / adapters.ts / actions.ts / index.ts (where applicable)
> â–، CACHE        Every data fn shared between page+generateMetadata is wrapped in React.cache
> â–، SHIM         Every consumer page.tsx â‰¤30 lines (no Firestore query in page)
> â–، INITIAL      Every detail page passes initialX to its view component (no double-fetch)
> â–، OG           Every detail route has opengraph-image.tsx as â‰¤30-line shim â†’ appkit renderer
> â–، NO-HARDCODE  No "LetItRip" / "letitrip.in" / currency / route strings inside _internal/
> â–، OPTS         Every public appkit function takes opts?: XOptions
> â–، SLOTS        Every appkit view accepts at least one renderXxx slot
> â–، EXPORTS      Server fns in server-entry.ts; client fns in client-entry.ts; no firebase-admin reachable from client-entry
> â–، NO-DUP       Run the Duplication Decision Framework on every cross-tier overlap
> ```

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| RA-Tier1 | Retrofit audit â€” Tier 1 Rich Text System | âڈ³ | |
| RA-Tier2 | Retrofit audit â€” Tier 2 Product Custom Fields & Detail Sections | âڈ³ | |

## Tier AK â€” Appkit Reusability + Provider-Registry DI *(post-beta)*

> Post-beta cleanup. Rewrites OK â€” no backwards-compat shims, no deprecation periods. Delete old code outright; change call sites in the same commit.

### â†’ Tier AK â€” *Phase 1: lifts from letitrip.in â†’ appkit*

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| AK1-typography | Create `appkit/src/features/typography/` with `<TypographyProvider>` + `<FontToggler>` + `useTypography()`. Pass font className map + localStorage key prefix from consumer. | âڈ³ | Migrates `src/components/user/FontToggleClient.tsx`. Default no-op so existing letitrip.in renders identically. |
| AK1-newsletter | Create `appkit/src/_internal/{client,server}/features/newsletter/` with `<NewsletterForm source="...">` + `INewsletterProvider` (`subscribe(email, source)`). letitrip.in registers Firestore-backed impl. | âڈ³ | Consolidates `HomepageNewsletterForm.tsx` + `FooterNewsletterSlot.tsx` (duplicate). Server `actions.ts` + Zod schema in `_internal/shared/features/newsletter/`. |
| AK1-logger | Move `src/lib/logger.ts` â†’ `appkit/src/monitoring/logger.ts`. Add `ILoggerProvider` contract in `appkit/src/contracts/logger.ts`. Export `getLogger()` via registry. | âڈ³ | Sits next to existing `error-tracking.ts` + `performance.ts`. Default console impl; consumer can register Cloud Logging / Sentry / NDJSON. |
| AK1-url-table | Inline letitrip's `useUrlTable` wrapper logic â€” accept `router?` + `pathname?` overrides in appkit's `useUrlTable` opts. Delete `src/hooks/useUrlTable.ts`. | âڈ³ | Verifies the `opts?` contract works end-to-end. |
| AK1-ui-labels | Extract generic `UI_LABELS` namespaces (LOADING, EMPTY, ACTIONS, ERROR, TABLE) â†’ `appkit/src/_internal/client/i18n/defaults.ts`. Wire into `LabelsProvider` defaults. letitrip.in keeps only brand-specific labels. | âڈ³ | ~200 lines moved. No consumer code changes â€” `LabelsProvider` falls back to defaults. |
| AK1-audit | One-shot scan of `letitrip.in/src/` for further generic candidates (search inputs, breadcrumbs, share buttons, copy-to-clipboard, useDebounce/useLocalStorage/useMediaQuery hooks). Produces follow-up rows under AK1. | âڈ³ | Audit only. Each finding â†’ its own row. |

### â†’ Tier AK â€” *Phase 2: DI seams for swappable features*

> Every feature below gets an `I<Feature>Provider` interface in `appkit/src/contracts/`, a default impl, and registration via `appkit/src/contracts/registry.ts`. Consumer registers its own impl at boot to replace any of them without forking appkit.

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| AK2-checkout-di | Add `ICheckoutProvider` contract: `createOrder(cart, address, payment)`, `validateCart(cart)`, `getSteps()`. Refactor `CheckoutView` to consume provider via `useCheckoutProvider()`. Keep current logic as `DefaultCheckoutProvider`. | âڈ³ | Flagship example. Cart stays in appkit untouched; checkout becomes consumer-replaceable. |
| AK2-cart-di | Add `ICartProvider` contract: `getCart()`, `addItem()`, `removeItem()`, `merge(guest, user)`, `clear()`. Cart hooks (`useCart`, `useAddToCart`) consume via provider. Default = current localStorage + Firestore impl. | âڈ³ | Lets consumer swap to Redis/server-cart without touching UI. |
| AK2-notification-di | Add `INotificationProvider` contract: `notify({type, title, body, userId, entityId})`. Default = Firestore `notifications` collection. Consumer can register FCM/email/webhook impl. | âڈ³ | Currently hardcoded to `notificationsRepository` everywhere. |
| AK2-media-upload-di | Add `IMediaUploadProvider` contract: `requestSignedUrl(ctx)`, `confirmUpload(slug)`, `abortUpload(slug)`. Default = current Firebase Storage signed-URL flow. | âڈ³ | Lets consumer swap to S3/Cloudinary/Bunny. `generateMediaFilename(ctx)` stays in appkit. |
| AK2-address-di | Add `IAddressValidationProvider` contract: `validate(address)`, `normalize(address)`, `geocode?(address)`. Default = pincode-only India validation. | âڈ³ | Currently inlined in `AddressForm`. |
| AK2-search-pluggable | `ISearchProvider` already exists in `contracts/search.ts` â€” audit `SearchView` to confirm it consumes via provider not direct repo calls. Fix gaps. | âڈ³ | Audit + retrofit. |
| AK2-copilot-classify | Audit `features/copilot/` â€” decide pure-client vs. provider-backed. If provider: add `ICopilotProvider`. | âڈ³ | Cross-links `X-copilot-classify`. |
| AK2-registry-doc | Document the full provider registry in `appkit/README.md` â€” every `I*Provider`, default impl, how to register a custom one. Include the 6-level Override Hierarchy. | âڈ³ | Cross-links `IX-override-doc` + `IX-appkit-docs`. |

### â†’ Tier AK â€” *Phase 3: SOLID + design-principles sweep*

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| AK3-srp-audit | **SRP** â€” flag any `_internal/server/features/<f>/data.ts` doing mutations (belongs in `actions.ts`) or `actions.ts` doing reads (belongs in `data.ts`). | âڈ³ | Punch-list output; each gap â†’ fix row under owning tier. |
| AK3-ocp-slots | **OCP** â€” every appkit view export accepts at least one `renderXxx` slot prop. Gaps become rows. | âڈ³ | Sister to lint rule `X-slots-lint`. |
| AK3-lsp-repo | **LSP** â€” any subclass overriding `BaseRepository` methods in a way that breaks the parent contract (e.g. `createWithId` bypass â€” recurrent pattern #9). | âڈ³ | Generate rows for each violator. |
| AK3-isp-contracts | **ISP** â€” split fat `I*Provider` contracts (>6 methods) into role-specific sub-contracts (e.g. `ICheckoutValidator` + `ICheckoutOrchestrator` + `ICheckoutPayment`). | âڈ³ | Apply to new AK2 contracts before they fossilize. |
| AK3-dip-direct-repo | **DIP** â€” every appkit component/hook importing a concrete repository instead of a provider. Each â†’ fix row. | âڈ³ | Structural enforcer for AK2. |
| AK3-opts-everywhere | Backfill `opts?: XOptions` on every appkit public function lacking it. Codified by `X-opts-lint`. | âڈ³ | |
| AK3-dry-duplication | **DRY** â€” run Duplication Decision Framework (CLAUDE.md) on every cross-feature overlap surfaced during AK1. | âڈ³ | Cross-links `IX-DUP-AUDIT`. |
| AK3-yagni-prune | **YAGNI** â€” flag any contract method / slot prop / opts field with **zero callers**. Delete or document a near-term consumer. | âڈ³ | |
| AK3-demeter | **Law of Demeter** â€” flag chains like `user.profile.settings.theme.color` deeper than 2 hops in appkit code. Introduce intermediate accessors. | âڈ³ | |
| AK3-composition | **Composition over Inheritance** â€” audit `appkit/src/repositories/` + `_internal/server/features/*/` class hierarchies. Anything â‰¥3 levels deep â†’ `mixin(BaseRepo, [WithPII, WithAudit, WithCache])`. | âڈ³ | |
| AK3-tell-dont-ask | **Tell-Don't-Ask** â€” flag controllers reading state then calling back (`if (cart.isEmpty()) cart.addItem(x)` â†’ `cart.addIfEmpty(x)`). | âڈ³ | Surfaces missing intent methods on providers. |

## Tier AP â€” Architectural Patterns (beyond DI) *(post-beta)*

> GoF / DDD / CQRS patterns either already informal in the codebase or that would materially simplify upcoming work. Each row formalizes one pattern with a clear seam.

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| AP1-strategy | **Strategy** â€” extract pluggable algorithms: `IPricingStrategy` (regular/auction/pre-order/bundle/prize-draw), `IDiscountStrategy` (percentage/fixed/free-shipping/BOGO), `IShippingRateStrategy` (flat/weight/Shiprocket). Default strategies via registry. | âڈ³ | Aligns with SB1 listingType migration. |
| AP2-adapter | **Adapter** â€” every `_internal/server/features/<f>/adapters.ts` must export `toClientX(doc)` + `fromClientX(payload)` symmetric pair. Codify naming + signature; lint rule `lir/require-adapter-pair`. | âڈ³ | Already partially in place. |
| AP3-facade | **Facade** â€” document that appkit barrels (`index.ts`, `client.ts`, `server.ts`) ARE facades. Nothing outside appkit may reach into `appkit/src/features/**` directly. Lint via `lir/no-deep-appkit-import` (extend existing `lir/no-deep-barrel-import`). | âڈ³ | |
| AP4-repository-decorator | **Decorator** â€” replace ad-hoc `BaseRepository` overrides (PII encryption, audit, caching) with composable `withPii(repo)` / `withAudit(repo)` / `withCache(repo)` decorators. Solves `createWithId` bypass class (recurrent #9). | âڈ³ | Pairs with `AK3-composition`. Each decorator one file in `appkit/src/repositories/decorators/`. |
| AP5-observer-eventbus | **Observer / Event Bus** â€” `appkit/src/events/` with typed channels: `orderPlaced`, `bidWon`, `productViewed`, `userBanned`. Replaces cross-feature direct chains (order â†’ notification â†’ email). | âڈ³ | Default in-process bus; consumer can bridge to pub/sub (FCM, Cloud Tasks). |
| AP6-command-action | **Command** â€” every `"use server"` action follows `{ input: ZodSchema, handler: (input, ctx) => Result, name: string }` shape so they can be queued, retried, audited, replayed. Retrofit one feature at a time. | âڈ³ | Foundation for offline-queue + audit log. |
| AP7-cqrs-formalize | **CQRS-lite** â€” codify the existing `data.ts` (queries, `cache()`-wrapped) vs. `actions.ts` (commands) split. Lint rule `lir/no-cross-cqrs-call`. | âڈ³ | Sister to `AK3-srp-audit`. |
| AP8-state-machine | **State Machine** â€” formalize lifecycles for order (PENDINGâ†’PROCESSINGâ†’SHIPPEDâ†’DELIVEREDâ†’REFUNDED), auction (DRAFTâ†’LIVEâ†’ENDEDâ†’SETTLED), pre-order (TAKING_ORDERSâ†’AWAITING_STOCKâ†’FULFILLINGâ†’CLOSED), ban (NONEâ†’SOFTâ†’HARD), event-entry (PENDINGâ†’CONFIRMEDâ†’CANCELLEDâ†’WAITLISTED). Use lightweight custom FSM or `xstate`. | âڈ³ | Replaces scattered `if (status === "X" && newStatus === "Y") allow`. |
| AP9-specification | **Specification** â€” composable Firestore filters: `new ActiveListingsSpec().and(new InCategorySpec(slug)).and(new PriceBetweenSpec(lo, hi))`. Existing sieve is partial impl. | âڈ³ | Bridges sieve params (f/s/p/ps/q) to typed predicates. |
| AP10-builder-order | **Builder** â€” `new OrderBuilder().forBuyer(uid).fromCart(cart).withAddress(addr).withCoupon(code).withPaymentMethod(razorpay).build()`. Replaces the current 60-line `createOrder()`. Validation at `build()`. | âڈ³ | Used inside `DefaultCheckoutProvider`. |
| AP11-chain-of-resp | **Chain of Responsibility** â€” checkout pipeline: validateCart â†’ applyDiscounts â†’ computeShipping â†’ computeTax â†’ reserveInventory â†’ createPayment â†’ persistOrder â†’ notify. Each link independently testable, registrable, replaceable. | âڈ³ | Pairs with AP1 (strategies) + AP6 (commands). |
| AP12-null-object | **Null Object** â€” every `I*Provider` ships a `NoOpXProvider` default so consumers opt out without registering. Remove `?.` chains in callers. | âڈ³ | E.g. `NoOpLoggerProvider`, `NoOpNotificationProvider`. |
| AP13-template-method | **Template Method** â€” `BaseRepository` already uses this. Audit + document hook points (`beforeCreate`, `afterCreate`, `beforeUpdate`) so subclasses don't bypass via direct field writes. Pair with AP4 decorators. | âڈ³ | |
| AP14-memento-draft | **Memento** â€” formalize draft-save / undo for admin forms (product editor, blog editor, carousel slide builder). One `useDraft(key, snapshot)` hook in appkit. | âڈ³ | Each form currently rolls its own localStorage save. |
| AP15-composite-sections | **Composite** â€” homepage sections + carousel + product custom sections are composite trees. Document `ISectionRenderer` contract so new section types plug in without touching `HomepageRenderer` switch. | âڈ³ | Replaces the 21-section-type switch. Open/Closed for sections. |
| AP16-principles-doc | Add `appkit/docs/architecture.md` â€” one page per pattern with when to use, when NOT, code example, anti-example, related rules. Index from `appkit/README.md`. | âڈ³ | Onboarding artifact. |

| # | Task | Status | Notes |

| LP1-audit-violations | Migrate `appkit/scripts/audit-violations.mjs` â†’ `lir/no-internal-boundary-cross` rule. Enforces `_internal/{client,shared,server}` cross-import bans currently in `appkit/.eslintrc.json` + script. | âڈ³ | Delete script after rule lands + `package.json` `check:audits` updated. |
| LP1-verify-entries | Migrate `appkit/scripts/verify-entries.mjs` â†’ `lir/no-firebase-admin-in-client-entry` rule. Walks import graph from `appkit/src/client.ts` / `client-entry.ts`. | âڈ³ | Already partly covered by `lir/no-firebase-admin-outside-backend`; this is the entry-graph variant. |
| LP1-audit-ssr | Migrate `scripts/audit-ssr-in-appkit.mjs` â†’ 4 rules: `lir/enforce-ssr-shim-size` (â‰¤30 line page.tsx), `lir/enforce-ssr-sidecar` (data.ts/adapters.ts present), `lir/no-hardcoded-branding-in-internal`, `lir/no-fat-og-image` (â‰¤40 line opengraph-image.tsx). | âڈ³ | Baseline of 8 root violations becomes `warn` for grandfathered files; new files `error`. Cross-links `X-audit-baseline`. |
| LP1-verify-css-keep | Keep `appkit/scripts/verify-css-build.mjs` as-is (post-build artifact check; not lintable). | âڈ³ | Marker row documenting the decision. |

### â†’ Tier LP â€” *Phase 2: new rules from CLAUDE.md anti-patterns*

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| LP2-listing-type | `lir/no-isauction-isPreorder-boolean` â€” flag any read/write of `isAuction` / `isPreOrder` on a product. Use `isAuctionListing(p)` / `normalizeListingType(p)`. Codifies SB1-G Phase 4 (recurrent #1). | âڈ³ | Medium. Property-access + object-key + import-name checks. |
| LP2-no-raw-hex | `lir/no-raw-hex-color` â€” flag `#[0-9a-fA-F]{3,8}` in `style={}` props and `*.css` outside variable defs. Use `var(--appkit-color-*)`. | âڈ³ | Medium. |
| LP2-no-z-arbitrary | `lir/no-arbitrary-z-index` â€” flag `z-[N]` in className strings. Use `var(--appkit-z-*)`. | âڈ³ | Easy. |
| LP2-no-inline-nav | `lir/no-inline-nav-groups` â€” flag inline definition of `*_NAV_GROUPS` or sidebar nav arrays in layout files. Import from `@/constants/navigation`. | âڈ³ | Medium. |
| LP2-no-import-side-css | `lir/no-css-at-import-from-node-modules` â€” flag `@import "@mohasinac/*"` in `globals.css`. Forces JS `import "pkg/styles"` in `layout.tsx`. Codifies recurrent #10. | âڈ³ | Easy. CSS-AST rule. |
| LP2-routes-strict | `lir/no-hardcoded-route` enhancement â€” extend to cover `redirect()`, `permanentRedirect()`, `Link href={\`/x/${id}\`}`, fetch URLs. | âڈ³ | Enhances existing rule. |
| LP2-media-filename | `lir/require-generate-media-filename` â€” flag string literals matching `firebasestorage.googleapis.com` written to Firestore docs. Use `generateMediaFilename(ctx)` + `/media/<slug>` proxy. | âڈ³ | Medium. |
| LP2-no-bare-fetch-firestore | `lir/no-direct-firestore-write` â€” flag `setDoc`/`updateDoc`/`addDoc` outside `appkit/src/repositories/` + `_internal/server/features/*/actions.ts`. | âڈ³ | Enhances `lir/no-direct-firestore-query`. |
| LP2-opts-suffix | `lir/require-opts-param` (codifies `X-opts-lint`) â€” flag any export from appkit facades whose last parameter is not `opts?:` and has â‰¥1 parameter. | âڈ³ | Hard. Public-export crawl. |
| LP2-render-slot | `lir/require-render-slot-prop` (codifies `X-slots-lint`) â€” flag any appkit view-shell export whose props don't include at least one `render*` prop. | âڈ³ | Hard. Component-prop type check. |
| LP2-firebase-admin-static | `lir/no-static-firebase-admin-import` â€” flag top-level `import` of `firebase-admin/*` outside `appkit/src/server.ts` + `_internal/server/**` + `repositories/**`. Codifies Turbopack client-bundle trap. | âڈ³ | Medium. |
| LP2-sideEffects-flag | `lir/require-sideeffects-false` â€” package.json rule on `appkit/package.json`: `"sideEffects": false` must remain. Without it Turbopack bundles firebase-admin chain. | âڈ³ | Easy. JSON rule. |
